American and Japanese Representatives Arrive in England, Naval Preparatory Conference to Resume, Britain and America Await Japanese Proposals, Conference Prospects Uncertain 35

(London) Whether the preparatory talks for the 1935 Naval Conference can begin before next week remains uncertain. These preparatory talks should begin with the Japanese delegation. Britain and America are awaiting the proposals of the Japanese representatives. Before the Japanese proposals are submitted, the preparatory work of the British and American delegations is futile. Most of this week will be spent by Japanese representative Rear Admiral Yamamoto and Japanese Ambassador to the UK Matsudaira to coordinate everything. Before the Japanese delegation is ready, Anglo-Japanese negotiations will not begin, let alone anything else. (Havas, 16th)

(London) The United States and Japan have sent representatives to London for preliminary negotiations for the naval conference. Japan's representative is Rear Admiral Yamamoto, who recently passed through the United States. The United States' representatives are Norman Davis, who has participated in disarmament conferences in the past, and Chief of Naval Operations Stanley, who also departed eastward a few days ago. British officials are taking a wait-and-see attitude before the representatives of both countries arrive. Japan's Rear Admiral Yamamoto will arrive in London tomorrow morning. Upon arrival, he will contact the Japanese Ambassador to the UK, Matsudaira, to convey the instructions of the Japanese government. The American representative, Davis, will disembark at Plymouth Harbor tomorrow night and will confer with the American Ambassador to the UK, Bingham, to discuss the attitude that the American representative should adopt. After the representatives of the two countries each contact their respective ambassadors, preliminary naval negotiations can begin. However, the bilateral nature of the talks will be strictly maintained. In other words, there will be separate talks between Britain and Japan, the United States and Japan, and Britain and the United States, rather than a joint consultation between the representatives of the three countries. Because the official naval conference is scheduled for next year, holding a joint meeting of representatives from the three countries during the preliminary talks would give the impression that the naval conference is being held prematurely. Separate talks can avoid this problem. The scope of the Japanese proposal is currently unknown. Before the Japanese proposal is announced, the British side will temporarily be represented by First Lord of the Admiralty, Sir Bolton Eyres Monsell, and will not express a specific direction for the talks, but will wait for Japan to put forward its suggestions before determining the British viewpoint. According to the official declarations made by Tokyo regarding Japan's naval policy, which have sometimes seemed contradictory, Japan's desire to abolish the Washington Naval Treaty cannot be denied. The abolition of the naval treaty has two implications: (1) the issue of naval bases in the Far East will be raised again; (2) political issues will be mixed into naval technology and strategy. In this way, countries with political demands will gain entry into the 1935 Naval Conference. It is generally believed that if the naval conference develops to this point, Britain will not oppose the participation of secondary naval powers in the naval conference, and political issues will inevitably be raised. As for the issue of naval ratios, Britain does not see how it can accept Japan's request to revise the original 5:5:3 ratio of the Washington Naval Treaty. Britain believes that the ratio system was adopted primarily to ensure national security, not just for national prestige. Moreover, countries have different types and sizes of overseas territories, and the government's responsibility for protection and the extent to which it needs the navy also vary. The ratio system is determined in light of these circumstances. (Havas, 15th)

Only a dozen people are guarding them, while the remaining workers have been transferred to Stone Village and Puyang to deal with the flood risk. (Special Dispatch, 16th)

Wang is scheduled to leave Guangdong and return north on the 18th. (Special Dispatch, 16th)

Increased Penalties for Grave Robbers 52

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Military Affairs issued an order to all military agencies yesterday, stating that cases of grave robbing have been rampant in various parts of Hebei in recent years. Some people have even made a living by digging up graves and stealing burial objects. If they are still sentenced to imprisonment according to criminal law, it is not enough to appease public outrage. In the future, any bandit caught carrying weapons to rob graves, or who makes a living from robbing graves, shall be sentenced to life imprisonment. Those who commit violence against tomb keepers and openly rob, or those who conspire with three or more people and rob graves while holding guns, shall be sentenced to death. Ordinary cases of grave robbery will still be dealt with according to criminal law. This has been approved by the Executive Yuan and filed with the Central Political Council, ordering all subordinates to be informed. (Special Dispatch, 16th)

Mutiny of Soldiers in Zhongshan County, Guangdong 83

County Soldiers Riot for Pay, Kidnap Chief of Public Security Bureau

Tang Shaoyi Suffers Shock, Mental Confusion Ensues

Guangzhou Correspondence: Tang Shaoyi, the model county magistrate of Zhongshan and standing committee member of the Southwest Political Affairs Council, has recently become unpopular with a segment of the population. The movement to overthrow Tang has been brewing for a long time. Several months ago, representatives of the citizens of Zhongshan County enumerated Tang's ten major crimes and came to the province to accuse Tang to the military and political authorities. Later, Tang was able to get the case against him temporarily suspended through the influence of some people. However, those who opposed Tang did not give up. Soon after, there was an assassination attempt on Tang at his home. Fortunately, Tang's guards repelled several assassins, although two guards were killed. Tang was unharmed. Recently, Lin Shuwei, the chief of the Zhongshan County Public Security Bureau, resigned voluntarily. In order to suppress the situation, Tang urgently appointed his trusted confidant Lin Jinghun as the chief of the Public Security Bureau and a Mr. Xiao as the head of the county soldiers. However, the organization and strength of the Zhongshan County police force are concentrated in the Public Security Bureau, which controls all county soldiers, police, and security teams, possessing approximately 10,000 firearms. The county soldiers are organized into three battalions, each with three companies, each company divided into three platoons. Each battalion has a strength of 1,000 soldiers. With Lin Shuwei's resignation as chief of the Public Security Bureau, the position became fiercely contested by both sides. The order appointing Lin Jinghun to replace him further incited Tang's opponents. Therefore, soon after Lin Jinghun received Tang's order but before he took office, the county soldiers, using the pretext of unpaid wages, started a dispute, swarming to Tang Shaoyi's residence in Tangjiawan, binding up Lin Jinghun, and threatening Tang with weapons, forcing him to hand over county administration. Tang, nearing seventy years old,

was so frightened that his face turned pale and his mind became deranged. The mutinous soldiers then escorted Lin Jinghun back to Shiqi, plunging the entire county into a state of anarchy. This occurred on the 5th of this month. The county party headquarters and county council jointly selected four representatives on the 6th to petition the province to maintain order in the county. The highest military authorities immediately dispatched Liang Gongfu's battalion from Luo Cequn's regiment of the First Training Division to Zhongshan to maintain county security. After arriving in the province, the Zhongshan citizen representatives also consulted with the headquarters, provincial government, and the Southwest Political Affairs Rehabilitation Committee to inquire about solutions. The various agencies did not give specific answers for the time being. Currently, the newly appointed chief of the Public Security Bureau, Lin Jinghun, is being held captive, and Tang Shaoyi is bedridden. The position of county magistrate is therefore vacant. The military authorities plan to temporarily appoint Luo Cequn, the regimental commander of the Training Division sent to Zhongshan to maintain security, to act as county magistrate, and Liang Gongfu, the battalion commander, as the acting chief of the Public Security Bureau. The impact of this incident on Tang's elderly and frail body is particularly detrimental. Hu Hanmin, residing in Hong Kong, heard the news and wired Chen Jitang yesterday, instructing him to protect Tang, stating: "I heard that a major dispute has broken out in Zhongshan. The specific situation is not very clear here, but since Shao Lao (Tang Shaochuan) is in a dangerous position, the provincial troops should be ordered to disband the rebellious county soldiers and ensure Shao Lao's safety in the province as the first priority. This is our responsibility, both publicly and privately." (9th)

Reuters Special Commercial News, October 16th 84

(Gold and Silver) ▲London Gold Price: The London gold price this morning was 142 shillings and 9.5 pence, down 3.5 pence.

▲Bombay Silver Bar: The Bombay silver market is stable. The spot price is 67 rupees and 10 annas, the November price is 67 rupees and 11 annas, each up 6 annas, and the December price is up 7 annas, at 67 rupees and 15 annas.

Also, 1 US dollar equals 4 shillings and 0.775 pence in British currency.

▲British-French: The opening rate this morning was 73 francs and 90 centimes, down 6 pounds. It did not rise until 2:00 PM, when it rose by 13 pounds to 74 francs and 03 centimes.

The National Army Recovers Xingguo City 86

Heavy Casualties for the Pseudo 15th Army Corps

National Army Pursues Remnants Towards Ningdu

Nanchang Correspondence: Xingguo is located in the western part of southern Jiangxi Province. To the east, it is parallel to Ningdu and Shicheng, to the west, it depends on Taihe and Wan'an, to the north, it connects to important bandit lairs such as Donggu, Futian, Longgang, Wangpi, and Xiaopu in Yongfeng, Jishui, Ji'an, and Ningdu, and to the south, it serves as a barrier for the bandit areas of Yudu and Ganzhou. It is a stronghold for bandits on both the east and west banks of the Gan River. Previously, when the Northern Route Army recovered Guangchang, Xingguo, Shicheng, and Ningdu were aligned. From a military standpoint, they should be listed as simultaneous targets. Furthermore, because the bandits in southeastern Jiangxi were heavily surrounded by the National Army, there was a trend for them to break out of the encirclement from Xingtai and Wan'an across the Gan River and flee westward to Hunan and Guizhou. Therefore, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek specifically ordered Zhou Hunyuan to lead troops to station in Taihe to capture Xingguo and to strengthen the defense forces in the middle section of the Gan River to block the bandits' westward escape route. This involved dozens of battles, large and small, the most notable of which were the battles of Shacun, Lantian, and Laopan. These locations were all dangerous mountainous areas where the bandits had already built strong fortifications with stone bunkers, earthen pits, trenches, and barricades that were very well-built. They were all broken through by the joint efforts of the National Army's infantry, artillery, and air forces. Another example is the battle of Gaoxingxu. This area is the heart of Xingguo and is related to the bandits' survival. In the bandit suppression campaign of the 20th year of the Republic, tens of thousands of bandits were killed in this battle, making it a famous battlefield in the history of bandit suppression, even more so than Jinggang, Jinjiazhai, and Qiliping. The Red bandits learned their lesson and deployed the pseudo 1st Army Corps, 1st, 2nd divisions, the pseudo 5th Army Corps, the 13th Independent 6th Division, and local pseudo-independent regiments in the highlands around Shixingshan, Zhugaoshan, and Shacunnao, attempting to fight the National Army. Starting on the 30th of last month, the National Army first launched a fierce bombing campaign with artillery and aircraft, followed by an infantry assault, destroying more than 30 bandit fortresses and killing thousands of bandits. On the 7th of this month, the National Army finally occupied Gaoxingxu. The bandits retreated to the county seat. After being relentlessly pursued by the National Army, they launched a siege on the 11th. At that time, the bandits in the city had completely lost their morale and were unable to fight any longer. They forced the people to destroy their stoves and break their pots, packing food and fleeing into the mountains. Taking advantage of the bandits' panic, the National Army launched a fierce attack and entered the county seat around 1 PM on the 15th. According to a phone call from the front, the pseudo 1st and 5th Army Corps suffered extremely heavy casualties and retreated toward Ningdu via the Longgangtou (northern Xingguo) area. They are still being pursued. Xingguo was captured by the bandits six or seven years ago. It was recovered once in the 20th year of the Republic, but was then reoccupied by the bandits. Hao Mengling's troops all made heroic sacrifices there, because the mountainous terrain made it difficult to recover. Now, the National Army has recovered it by proceeding step by step and building roads and bunkers. Wherever the army goes, order is stable. Xie Shouru, the magistrate of Xingguo County, who was handling post-war affairs in Lantian, has already entered the city with the army. The National Army is now clearing the battlefield, burying bandit corpses, repairing the city walls, constructing fortifications on the high ground attached to the city, and recruiting refugees. The main force is pursuing the bandits in order to wipe them out completely. (October 14th)

Robbery on the Zhangsong Road in Fujian Province 87

Bandits Impersonate Soldiers, Intercept Vehicles Halfway to Commit Robbery

After the Robbery, Five Passengers Were Kidnapped, Their Whereabouts Unknown

Xiamen Correspondence: On Double Tenth Day (October 10th), a passenger car on the Zhangsong Highway, a major transportation artery between Xiamen and Zhangzhou, was intercepted by bandits dressed as soldiers, and five passengers were kidnapped. The Zhangsong Road is 100 li long. Every day, steamships from the Xiamen station and express trains from the Zhangzhou station run ten round trips each. A slow train stops at small stations along the way every hour. At 9:00 AM on the morning of the 10th, the third express train from Zhangzhou to Xiamen, numbered Min Zi 1281, driver Hu Jianzhong, was traveling when four people suddenly blocked the road with Browning pistols as the car reached Donghu Township, 25 li from Zhangzhou. The driver tried to accelerate past, but the men opened fire, the bullets grazing the side of the car. The driver thought they were regular soldiers and had no way to avoid them, so he stopped the car. Only then did the driver and passengers realize they had encountered bandits, but they were helpless. The bandits forced the driver to continue driving towards Songyu. Two more bandits boarded the car after passing Zhentou, and two more boarded after passing Jiangdong Bridge, all dressed as soldiers. Upon reaching Cai Dian, the bandits ordered the car to stop and searched the passengers' belongings. All 25 passengers in the car were searched. After the search, they left five passengers on the car and drove the rest off, forcing the driver and the five passengers to huddle under the seats in the car, not allowing them to move. One bandit drove the car, four bandits held Browning pistols, standing on the left and right sides, while the two bandits holding onto the car were on guard, and the remaining three bandits held guns in the car, monitoring the five passengers and the driver, strictly forbidding them from making any noise. The bandits spoke in a Nanyang "Malay" dialect and spoke to each other in Cantonese or English. After driving the car themselves, the bandits immediately accelerated and sped to Jiaowei. Jiaowei Station is one of the stations on the Zhangsong Line, 30 li from Songyu, and is also the starting station for the Jiaotong Line (Jiaowei to Tong'an). Troops are stationed there. The bandit car drove to the station without stopping and turned east towards the Jiaotong Line. The sentries at the station wanted to come forward to inquire, but the bandit car had already turned and sped away. The sentries and staff at the Jiaowei Station of the Zhangsong Line thought it was a passenger car requisitioned by the military. However, the platoon leader stationed at Jiaodong found it strange that the car did not stop for inspection and immediately inquired at Jiaowei Station and contacted Zhangzhou Station by telephone, only to learn that it had been robbed by bandits. After being informed, the Zhangsong Management Department immediately sent people to Jiaowei and consulted with the fourth company of the Tong'an Ninth District Security Corps stationed in Dongpu Township. The military and security corps jointly dispatched a team to pursue them. At that time, the driver Hu Jianzhong had escaped and returned, driving the original car back to Jiaowei. He then used the original car to carry the fourth company of the Security Corps to pursue them, but the bandits had already fled far away. According to Hu Jianzhong, after the bandits drove the car past the Jiaowei sentry line, they sped along the Jiaotong Line towards Guankou. They stopped at the Guanyin Temple in Guankou, about 27-28 li from Jiaowei. First, they tied him to telephone pole number 709 on the side of the road with a hemp rope, then drove the five kidnapped passengers over the Yangkeng and Shenkeng Mountains. After the bandits left, a passing cowherd untied him, and he drove the original car back, according to the report. When the fourth company of the Security Corps arrived at the scene by car, nearby villagers said that the bandits had fled into the mountains long ago, seemingly heading towards Changtai or Lotus Mountain. The corps members immediately returned to Zhangzhou to report. After the Zhangzhou City Defense Command received the report from the garrison in Jiaowei, it ordered the temporary detention of the car driver Hu Jianzhong for questioning on the 11th. It also dispatched a team to patrol the Zhangsong Line from 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM and ordered another team to search Tong'an. As of the evening of the 11th, nothing had been found. Only one of the five kidnapped passengers is known to be named Lu Lian, an employee of the Zhangzhou MSG factory. The names of the other four passengers have not yet been verified. The bandits speak Malay, Cantonese, and English, and seem to be returning overseas Chinese or Cantonese bandits. (12th)

(Songjiang)

A New Twist in the Theft Case in Xinzhuang 88

The Peng family of Peng Fusheng in Xinzhuang is of ordinary means, barely making ends meet. This year's drought resulted in a poor harvest. Recently, the cotton matured, and they harvested twelve bales of cotton, intending to sell them to clear their old debts. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 13th, thieves stole all twelve bales of cotton. The owner was terrified. It was later learned that the culprits were Zhang Aliang and Lu Yongquan. Zhang Yongquan is related to Peng Fusheng through marriage. The stolen cotton was jointly owned by Peng Fusheng and his sister-in-law, a certain Ms. Peng. Upon hearing about the theft, Peng Fusheng's sister-in-law was inconsolable. She lamented her fate and hanged herself in secret. The owner has reported the matter to the Sixth Sub-Station, which has arrested Zhang Aliang and Zhang Yongquan and handed them over to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation. However, the suicide of Peng Fusheng's sister-in-law due to the theft is a separate matter. It is unknown how this theft case will be resolved.

(Suzhou)

Chamber of Commerce Requests Correction of Stamp Tax Law 89

The Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce, in light of the recent stamp tax law passed by the Legislative Yuan, which sets excessively high tax rates that merchants cannot afford, specially submitted a proposal to the joint meeting of directors and supervisors on the 15th by Chairman Shi. Yesterday (the 16th), they telegraphed the National Government, the Central Political Committee, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry, appealing for a correction to alleviate the burden, citing the real situation where merchants are unable to bear the burden.

Zhang Da Appointed Deputy Division Commander 90

Zhang Da, an inspector of police affairs for the Department of Civil Affairs, was ordered to inspect police affairs in Wuxian County. Since arriving in Suzhou, Zhang has conducted thorough on-site inspections, paying particular attention to academic subjects. Many police chiefs who were examined by Zhang were either dismissed or promoted. The inspections of the three sub-bureaus in the urban area have been completed, and he is now inspecting rural areas such as Zai Zhi Chefang and Chenmu Township. It is expected to be completed in about ten days. It is also learned that Zhang Da has now been appointed as the deputy division commander of the 89th Division by the Ministry of Military Affairs.

County Magistrate Handles Opium Offenders Under Military Law 91

After the Opium Suppression Association stopped registration, 49 unregistered opium smokers, including Ding Zhifang, were arrested successively and are currently detained in the county government, awaiting investigation. Yesterday (the 16th), the county government received an order from the Zhenjiang Garrison Command to handle the cases of opium offenders under military law by the county magistrate. In addition, eight opium traffickers, including Shen Liusheng, are scheduled to be transferred to the Provincial Security Office for investigation today (the 17th). The Wuxian County Opium Prohibition Center was established yesterday (the 16th), currently with 100 personnel, divided into three classes.

(Wuxi)

Investigation of Liquor Tax Arouses Villagers 92

The Yizhong Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office, considering that there are over a thousand households distilling liquor in the New Third District, and the collected license fees over the years have been less than a quarter of the total, in order to rectify tax revenue and maintain the contracted amount, hired a boat and sent personnel to the district at the beginning of this month to investigate each liquor household, handle registration, and prepare to initiate the autumn license tax collection. Initially, the work was going smoothly, but unexpectedly, the night before, when the boat was docked in the river near Huadafang Village, more than a hundred villagers of unknown name suddenly came in the darkness, wielding bricks and stones, and violently attacked the boat, causing the boat windows to be shattered. The officials in the boat wrapped their heads in cotton blankets, preventing skin lacerations and bloodshed. Afterwards, they came to the city to report to the county government, which dispatched police to the countryside yesterday to arrest the perpetrators for legal action.

(Jiangyin)

Intense Riverbank Collapse at Lanmen Sandbar 93

The sandbar area from Zhangjiagang to the Lanmen Sandbar along the river has always been a region of intense riverbank collapse. In the 20th year of the Republic (1931), it suffered repeated major disasters. Farmers hoped to build dikes to protect against the collapse. The collapse intensified again the day before, with one enclosure collapsing at Mengjiangtang and two enclosures collapsing at Lanmen Sandbar. Several farmers and boats were also submerged. Currently, the three county offices for riverbank protection have been merged into the River Management Committee. The people of the sandbar all hope that the River Management Committee will formulate plans as soon as possible to comfort the sandbar residents.

(Zhenjiang)

Naval Captain Arrested for Smoking Opium 94

Liu Jicui, the captain of the Fuyan warship of the Second District of the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Public Security Team, a native of Nanchang, came to the province from his defense post on the 13th of this month to collect pay from the Finance Department. He stayed in a building at No. 17 Zhenping Mountain in this port and smoked opium. Yesterday afternoon, someone secretly reported the situation to the provincial government. After receiving the report, the provincial government sent personnel to inspect the address and found a complete set of smoking paraphernalia under the bed. A friend surnamed Liu, Mr. A, who was also staying in the room, was also arrested and temporarily detained by the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau for investigation.

(Yangzhou)

Third District Boy Scout Review Completed 95

The Third District Boy Scout Grand Review and Camp, which opened on the 11th, has been underway for five days. Various operations and course competitions have been completed one after another. It was originally scheduled to hold a joint Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week and closing ceremony at Meihan Middle School on the morning of the 15th, but due to the continuous rain, it was changed to the Yangxiang County Junior High School. The conference ended successfully. Chairman Zhou Shaocheng led the ceremony as scheduled, and then Tang Changyan, a representative of the Boy Scout General Association, gave a speech. Next, the chairman distributed souvenirs and other items. It is said that the total score of the competition will be officially announced today. Boy Scouts of both sexes from various counties have left the camp one after another. Due to transportation difficulties, it is reported that Huaiyin, Lianshui, Huaian and other counties will return to their counties when the weather clears.

(Changshu)

Fourth District Representatives Request Urgent Relief 96

This year's severe drought has caused a disaster, and the autumn harvest has been reduced. Each district has reported the yield to the county separately, especially the fifth and sixth districts, where the cotton fields are severely barren. However, in order to conduct an on-site inspection of the actual situation, the provincial departments have sent Shu Sheyu, Zhang Buzhou, and others to Changshu for inspection. It is now known that in the western Fourth District, due to the higher terrain, there was no way to draw water during the prolonged drought, so as much as five-tenths of the rice paddies were not planted. As a result, there is no hope for the autumn harvest. On the 15th, representatives Tang Guanghan, Miao Zuolin, Qian Yuanlong, and eight or nine others were dispatched to the county at 1 p.m. to visit the county magistrate and petition. They were immediately received, and the representatives made two requests: (1) Request the provincial inspection committee to visit the villages for inspection immediately; (2) Request the county magistrate to find a way to allocate funds immediately to handle urgent relief, because many farmers who did not plant rice have no harvest and are now sitting and waiting to die, otherwise they may take desperate risks. County Magistrate Zhai immediately stated that regarding the former, since the provincial committee has already come to Changshu, they can go to the villages for inspection immediately. Regarding the latter, he will do his best to provide relief, but a meeting must be held to discuss and find a solution in terms of economics.

(Hangzhou)

Verdict in Car Accident Killing Three People 97

Wang Xiang, the driver of the Hangzhou Public Welfare Automobile Company, was driving a freight car to Pengjiabu when he negligently ran over and killed three people, including the villager Wang Jinmu, his wife, and their three-year-old daughter. After being sent to the Hangzhou District Court for trial, Wang Xiang was sentenced yesterday to two years in prison for the crime of negligently causing death.

(Ningbo)

Basic Squad Uncovers Bandit Den 98

Shi Fulin, the captain of the Independent Second Squad of the Basic Squad of Xiaonü Township in the Fifth District of Yuyao, received a secret report at about 1 p.m. on the 13th, stating that a large number of kidnappers were hiding in the homes of Wu Demei and Wu Jinfu in Langhai Township, Yangdingqiu. Upon receiving the report, the captain immediately supervised his squad members and rushed to the address to ambush and arrest them. They successfully captured the bandits Qian Dabing, Wang Banglian, and Qian Xiao'abing, and seized a wooden-cased gun, eleven bullets, a four-inch White Wave Order pistol, twelve bullets, a six-inch White Wave Order pistol, and a large bag of clothes. They were sent to the Yuyao County Government for interrogation along with the harborers Wu Demei and Wu Wangshi.

Manager of Qian Zhuang Kidnapped and Escapes Danger 99

Huang Junrong, the manager of Zhixia Qian Zhuang under the Zhuangyuan Bridge in Dinghai, returned to his hometown of Duntou to drink wine for his cousin's wedding the day before (the 12th). Unexpectedly, at about 12 o'clock at night, four thieves suddenly came and kidnapped him. After being kidnapped to Xintang, about two li away from Duntou, the thieves had prepared a boat in advance, so they went down to the boat and landed on the Zhushan Bamboo Bay, climbed over mountains and ridges. Because Huang's feet were injured, he could no longer walk, so they rested temporarily in the pine forest on Shangze Mountain. Later, near Zhongze, they saw a small wheel coming, and the thieves suspected it was a pursuit force, so they released Huang and fled. Soon, a woodcutter passed by the area, and Huang told him the details of his ordeal. The woodcutter hired a boat to send him back, so he was able to escape danger. It can be said that he was lucky.

Special Report

The Constitution of the Republic of China Passed by the Legislative Yuan in the Third Reading 100

The draft constitution consisting of twelve chapters and one hundred and seventy-eight articles, drafted by the Legislative Yuan, was discussed in multiple consecutive sessions of the Legislative Yuan and was fully passed yesterday (16th) in the third reading. The revised full text is recorded below:

The National Assembly of the Republic of China, entrusted by all the people, and in accordance with the teachings of Mr. Sun Yat-sen, the founder of the Republic of China, hereby enacts this Constitution to be promulgated throughout the country, and shall always faithfully abide by it.

Chapter I: General Principles 101

Article 1: The Republic of China is a Republic based on the Three Principles of the People.

Article 2: The sovereignty of the Republic of China belongs to the entire people.

Article 3: Those who possess the nationality of the Republic of China are citizens of the Republic of China.

Article 4: The territory of the Republic of China consists of the inherent territories of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, Xikang, Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, Guizhou, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe, Chahar, Suiyuan, Ningxia, Xinjiang, Mongolia, and Tibet.

The territory of the Republic of China may not be altered without a resolution of the National Assembly.

Article 5: All ethnic groups within the Republic of China are constituent members of the Chinese nation and are equal.

Article 6: The national flag of the Republic of China is a blue sky and white sun in the upper left corner of a red field.

Article 7: The national capital of the Republic of China is Nanjing.

Chapter II: Rights and Duties of the People 102

Article 8: All citizens of the Republic of China are equal before the law.

Article 9: The people shall have freedom of person. No one may be arrested, detained, interrogated, or punished except in accordance with the law.

A person who is arrested or detained on suspicion of a crime shall be informed immediately by the executing agency of the reasons for the arrest or detention, as well as his or her relatives, and shall be transferred to the competent court for interrogation within twenty-four hours at the latest. The person or others may also petition the competent court to order the executing agency to produce the person for interrogation within twenty-four hours.

The court shall not reject the petition referred to in the preceding paragraph, nor shall the executing agency reject the court's order to produce the person.

Article 10: The people, except for active-duty military personnel, shall not be subject to military trial.

Article 11: The people shall have freedom of residence. Their residences may not be entered, searched, or sealed except in accordance with the law.

Article 12: The people shall have freedom of movement. It may not be restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 13: The people shall have freedom of speech, writing, and publication. It may not be restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 14: The people shall have freedom of secret communication. It may not be restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 15: The people shall have freedom of religious belief. It may not be restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 16: The people shall have freedom of assembly and association. It may not be restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 17: The property of the people may not be requisitioned, expropriated, sealed, or confiscated except in accordance with the law.

Article 18: The people shall have the right to petition, appeal, and litigate in accordance with the law.

Article 19: The people shall have the right to elect, recall, initiate, and referendum in accordance with the law.

Article 20: The people shall have the right to take examinations in accordance with the law.

Article 21: The people shall have the duty to pay taxes in accordance with the law.

Article 22: The people shall have the duty to perform military service in accordance with the law.

Article 23: The people shall have the duty to perform public service in accordance with the law.

Article 24: All other freedoms and rights of the people that do not prejudice social order or the public interest shall be protected by the Constitution.

Article 25: Any law restricting the freedom or rights of the people shall be limited to what is necessary to safeguard national security, avoid imminent danger, maintain social order, or promote the public interest.

Article 26: Any public official who violates the law and infringes upon the freedom or rights of the people shall be liable for criminal and civil liability in addition to disciplinary action in accordance with the law. The injured people shall also be entitled to claim compensation from the state for the damages they have suffered in accordance with the law.

Chapter III: The National Assembly 103

Article 27: The National Assembly shall be composed of the following national representatives:

1. One representative shall be elected from each county and city and their equivalent areas, but for every 500,000 people exceeding 300,000, one additional representative shall be elected.

The county, city, and equivalent areas shall be determined by law.

2. Representatives shall be elected from Mongolia and Tibet, and the number of representatives shall be determined by law.

3. Representatives shall be elected from citizens residing abroad, and the number of representatives shall be determined by law.

Article 28: The election of national representatives shall be conducted by means of universal, equal, direct, and secret ballot.

Article 29: Citizens of the Republic of China who have reached the age of twenty shall have the right to elect representatives in accordance with the law, and those who have reached the age of twenty-five shall have the right to be elected as representatives in accordance with the law.

Article 30: The term of office of national representatives shall be four years.

National representatives who violate the law or are derelict in their duties shall be recalled by their original electoral districts in accordance with the law.

Article 31: The National Assembly shall be convened once every two years, with a session of one month, which may be extended by one month if necessary.

With the consent of more than one-quarter of the representatives, the National Assembly may convene a special session of the National Assembly.

Article 32: The functions of the National Assembly are as follows: (1) To elect the President and Vice President, the President of the Legislative Yuan, the President of the Control Yuan, members of the Legislative Yuan, and members of the Control Yuan; (2) To recall the President and Vice President, the Presidents of the Legislative, Judicial, Examination, and Control Yuans, members of the Legislative Yuan, and members of the Control Yuan; (3) To initiate laws; (4) To referendum laws; (5) To amend the Constitution; (6) Other powers conferred by the Constitution.

Article 33: National representatives shall not be held responsible externally for their speeches and votes at meetings.

Article 34: Except in cases of flagrant crimes, national representatives may not be arrested or detained during the session without the permission of the National Assembly.

Article 35: The organization of the National Assembly and the election and recall of national representatives shall be determined by law. (To be continued)

Local News

He Yingqin Arrives in Shanghai from Nanjing Yesterday 104

He Talks About Tranquility in North China, Bandits Have Been Eliminated

Staying for a Week, Going to Nanjing, Returning North After the Fifth Plenary Session

He Yingqin, Minister of Military Administration and Chairman of the Peiping Military Branch, left Peiping southward a few days ago to pay respects to the passing of his mother-in-law, Madam Wang, and to attend the Fifth Plenary Session. He first met with Chairman Chiang, Chairman Lin, and President Wang. He arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing by night train the night before, and arrived at the North Station at 7:20 yesterday morning. Mayor Wu and others went to welcome him. Mr. He is scheduled to stay in Shanghai for a week and then return to Nanjing, and then return north after attending the Fifth Plenary Session. The details are as follows:

Welcome at the Station 105

Those who arrived at the North Station yesterday morning to welcome him included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of the Municipal Security Department Yang Hu, Secretary Jia Botao, Chief of Staff of the Songhu Garrison Command Xu Jinyuan, Yang Dezhao, representative of the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army Chen Jitang stationed in Nanjing, Miao Bin, former Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, and many of Mr. He's former subordinates, relatives, and friends in Shanghai.

Situation Upon Arrival 106

At 7:15, the train arrived at the North Station. The people who were welcoming him at the station immediately rushed to the side of the train to greet him. The military band of the Security Department also played music to welcome him. Mr. He and his entourage got off the train smiling amidst the melodious music and shook hands with the welcomers as a courtesy. After exchanging brief pleasantries, they walked out of the station together and changed to their own cars to return to their private residence on Avenue Joffre to rest. Yang Hu and Yang Dezhao also went to Mr. He's residence to talk briefly for a while before taking their leave. Mr. He was wearing a black-gray suit, a yellow leather overcoat, a black thin-striped tie, a velvet hat, and yellow leather shoes. He was as energetic as ever. Those who accompanied Mr. He to Shanghai yesterday morning included Xie Zhongyuan, Director of the Secretariat of the Ministry of Military Administration and Chief of the Confidential Group of the Peiping Military Branch, Hou Tianshi, Director of the Staff Department, Zhu Shiqin, Deputy Group Leader of the Fourth Group of the Military Branch, Lin Zhiqi, Secretary of the Ministry of Military Administration, Rao Chubai, Secretary of the Military Branch, and aide-de-camp Wang Guozhong.

Written Questions and Answers 107

After returning to his residence, Mr. He received reporters from various newspapers at around 8 o'clock and released written questions and answers as follows: (Question) How many former Northeast Army troops are currently in North China? How will they be handled? (Answer) All departments under the jurisdiction of the Military Branch are national troops and are not divided by the boundaries of the Northeast and Northwest. They are currently stationed in various places according to a fixed organization. (Question) Is there any possibility of transferring them south? (Answer) The bandit suppression force is sufficient, and there is no need to transfer them south again. (Question) What is the situation of pacification in North China? (Answer) The provinces of North China are now extremely stable, and the bandits in various places have been eliminated one after another this spring. (Question) How many days will you stay in Shanghai? After leaving Shanghai, will you visit Chairman Chiang again, or will you return north immediately? (Answer) I am here specifically to pay respects to Madam Wang, and after a week, I will return to Nanjing to inspect the agencies and army commanders directly under the Ministry of Military Administration. The return to the north is expected after the Fifth Plenary Session. (Question) Do you have any proposals for the Fifth Plenary Session? (Answer) I have no proposals for the Fifth Plenary Session.

Desiring Peace 108

In addition to answering the reporters' questions in writing, Mr. He also personally came out to talk with the reporters. It is said that the military situation for bandit suppression in Jiangxi is quite good. At this time of national crisis, it is hoped that the people of the country will unite as one and strive to become stronger. My long-cherished wish is to desire peace. When I went to Chahar and Suiyuan for inspection, I saw that many new houses had been built in the rural areas, and there had been significant progress in various constructions. The reason for this is that the area has not experienced war for more than a year, so the people can live and work in peace and engage in construction. This proves that only peace can promote construction. Our country is a member of the international community. If we want world peace, we must first seek domestic peace. Therefore, I, He Yingqin, sincerely hope that domestic peace will be realized as soon as possible, and then promote world peace, so that the mutual killing of mankind in the world can be avoided.

Mr. He Yingqin (neutral) taking a photo in Shanghai (photographed by Gong Shuxian)

Going to the Wang Residence 109

After receiving guests at his residence, Mr. He rested briefly and then, at around 10 a.m., accompanied by Secretary Xie Zhongyuan, Director Hou Tianshi, and others, took a car to the Wang residence on Yuyuan Road to pay respects to his mother-in-law, Madam Wang, and to offer condolences to his brother-in-law, former Minister of Communications Wang Boqun. He then stayed at the Wang residence for lunch, and did not leave until the afternoon. It is also known that Mayor Wu of this city will host a banquet for Mr. He within a few days to welcome him.

Silver Exports Gradually Cease After Imposition of Silver Export Tax 110

Gold Standard Price Soars by More Than Forty Yuan

More Than Twenty Million Silver Exported Last Week

According to the New News Agency, in order to prevent the continuous outflow of silver, our country has gradually reduced silver exports since the implementation of the silver export tax. The International Trade Bureau specially announced the total export volume last week yesterday. The details obtained yesterday are recorded as follows:

Customs Notice of Tax Collection 111

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and tax officer Boerder, jointly issued Notice No. 1389 yesterday morning, which stated: "Ordered by the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, the silver export tax rates are now formulated as follows: (1) Silver standard currency shall be subject to an export tax of 10%, minus the minting fee of 2.25%, resulting in a net tax of 7.75%; (2) Other types of silver shall be subject to an export tax of 10%. If the exchange rate of the London silver price converted to Shanghai exchange rate differs from the exchange rate determined by the Central Bank on the same day, the amount of the difference shall be paid in addition to the above-mentioned export tax. If there is still a shortfall, a balancing tax shall be levied according to the amount of the shortfall, which shall be implemented uniformly from the 15th of this month. All parties shall comply accordingly." It should be complied with accordingly. All batches of silver exported from the 15th of this month, regardless of the date of shipment, shall be taxed according to the new tax rate. All exporting merchants are hereby notified. This notice is hereby issued.

Exports Gradually Eliminated 112

Yesterday, a reporter from the New News Agency learned that foreign merchant ships preparing to ship silver for export, such as the Grand President of the Dollar Steamship Company, the Comorin of the British Company, and the Ikoma Maru of the Nippon Yusen Kaisha, contained a total of 9.25 million silver dollars. Among them, 1 million was taxed according to regulations and shipped to the United States. The silver owners and exporters felt that if they paid taxes according to the new tax rate, not only would there be no profit to be made, but they would also have to lose money, so they declared withdrawal from customs and suspended transportation. Therefore, no cash was shipped out yesterday. Since speculators generally have no profit to gain, they have all stopped their activities. It is predicted that silver exports can be gradually eliminated. The Customs specifically ordered the customs officers yesterday to conduct strict investigations to prevent smuggling.

Gold Standard Rises Sharply 113

Since the Ministry of Finance implemented the silver export tax, the gold standard market has continued to rise for days. However, the rise was even more severe yesterday. At 4:30 p.m., the closing price soared to more than 952.3 yuan, which is a phenomenon that has not been seen in recent times. The prices of yesterday are recorded below. The opening price in the morning was 914.3 yuan, the highest was 945 yuan, the lowest was 913.5 yuan, and the closing price was 944.8 yuan. The opening price in the afternoon was 952.5 yuan, the highest was 953 yuan, the lowest was 946 yuan, and the closing price was 952.3 yuan, an increase of more than 40 yuan compared to last week.

Investigation of Exports Last Week 114

The Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau announced yesterday that the total amount of silver exported from Shanghai from the 8th to the 13th of this month was more than 22 million yuan. The destinations and quantities are as follows: (1) Silver bars were shipped to Singapore for 6,900 yuan, London for 1,992,000 yuan, and San Francisco for 230,000 yuan; (2) Silver ingots were shipped to Kobe for 845,065.55 yuan, London for 600,751.33 yuan; (3) Silver dollars were shipped to London for 15,100,000 yuan, San Francisco for 770,000 yuan, Seattle for 500,000 yuan, Moji for 650,000 yuan, Hong Kong for 544,500 yuan, and Hong Kong foreign currency for 20,000 yuan.

Jiangsu Provincial Government Borrows 8 Million Yuan from Shanghai Banks and Qian Zhuang 115

Using Jiangsu Provincial Bonds of 15 Million Yuan as Collateral

Various Banks and Qian Zhuang Will Organize a Syndicate to Handle the Loan

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the 20 million yuan of Jiangsu Water Conservancy Construction Public Bonds in the 23rd year of the Republic of China (1934) were issued on October 1, they have already been printed. After arriving in Shanghai, Zhao Dihua, Director of the Finance Department, hosted a banquet for the leaders of Shanghai banks and qian zhuang the night before. Chen Zeqing, Ye Fuxiao, Lin Kanghou, and others from the banking industry, and Qin Runqing, Chairman of the Qian Industry Association, as the chief representative, attended. First, Director Zhao reported on the issuance of the Jiangsu Water Conservancy Construction Public Bonds, the use of the public bonds, and decided to organize a fund custody committee and invite the banking and qian industries to be members.

Contacting for Loans 116

During the banquet, Director Zhao contacted various banks such as the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Continental Bank, Yanyeh Bank, Jincheng Bank, Zhejiang Xingye Bank, Zhejiang Shiye Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Farmers Bank, and Agricultural and Commercial Bank, as well as various qian zhuang, and proposed to mortgage 8 million yuan with Jiangsu provincial bonds with a face value of 15 million yuan. Because the use of Jiangsu provincial bonds is for water conservancy construction, the banks and qian zhuang generally agreed in principle. Because it was a preliminary contact at the time, no specific decisions were made, and interest and term were not discussed. The banquet ended late at night.

Deciding to Form a Syndicate 117

Starting yesterday, Director Zhao has been contacting the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Continental Bank, Yanyeh Bank, Jincheng Bank, and other banks, as well as Qin Runqing, Chairman of the Qian Industry Association, to determine the amount of the loan. After each bank and qian zhuang determine the amount of the loan, they will hold a meeting to formally negotiate and decide. The various banks and qian zhuang have decided to form a syndicate to handle the loan in the future. The mortgage loan contract and all conditions will be negotiated and signed by the syndicate on behalf of the banks and qian zhuang with the Jiangsu Provincial Government.

The Social Affairs Bureau's Proclamation on Encouraging Labor-Management Harmony 122

Prohibiting Labor Unions from Forcing Workers to Join

Admonishing Businesses Not to Be Hostile Towards Labor Unions

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau issued Proclamation No. 9991 yesterday, stating that Article 20 of the Labor Union Law stipulates, "Labor unions shall not force workers to join or prevent them from withdrawing. Labor unions shall not refuse membership to those who are qualified under the law and articles of association, nor shall they allow membership to those who are unqualified. Labor unions shall not obstruct the work of non-union members." Article 31 of the same law stipulates, "Employers or their agents shall not refuse to employ or dismiss workers, or subject them to other unfavorable treatment, because they are members or officers of a labor union." Furthermore, Article 32 stipulates, "Employers or their agents shall not make non-participation in union duties, non-membership in a labor union, or withdrawal from a labor union a condition of employment." The above-mentioned articles of law have been repeatedly announced by this bureau. However, due to the passage of time, both labor and management still frequently cause disputes due to this, which is quite inappropriate. It must be understood that if the organization of a labor union can seek legitimate benefits for workers and make workers firm in their beliefs, why worry that they will not enthusiastically join? If they are hostile towards those who do not join, or even force them to join and hinder their work, this kind of immature behavior is the opposite of the purpose of organizing a union. Why should workers value such a labor union? On the employment side, it should be understood that labor unions are groups whose purpose is to increase workers' knowledge and skills, develop production, and maintain and improve labor conditions and living standards. If they are necessarily regarded as enemies of the capital side, or if the lack of organization and weak knowledge of the workers is used to take whatever one wants, and labor unions are regarded as superfluous, then suspicion will arise and the friendship of mutual assistance will be lost. Therefore, this proclamation is issued again earnestly, urging all labor unions, factories, and shops in this city to abide by it together and understand this purpose. If anyone dares to deliberately violate the law, this bureau will have to enforce the law and will never be lenient. This proclamation is imperative.

Two Cases of Rent Reduction for Landlords, Yongxing Lane and Renshun Lane Are Both Managed by Foreign Firms 123

(Yongxing Lane) Yongxing Lane, located at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Laobazi Road, is the property of Chen Bingqian, a wealthy Cantonese merchant, and is managed by Xiangmao Foreign Firm. Chen is a philanthropist, so the original rent was quite low. During the Shanghai war, the rent was reduced by 7%. Now, the tenants there, seeing that the market is in a slump and business is not improving, recently jointly submitted a letter requesting a further reduction. Most tenants are satisfied, which can be considered good news in the rent reduction movement.

(Renshun Lane) Renshun Lane Branch of the 26th District of the Municipal Federation, located on North Jiangxi Road, has been negotiating with Wuhe Foreign Firm since its establishment to promote rent reduction. The firm is acting as an agent. The landlord, seeing the market depression, agreed to a 10% rent reduction for the sake of maintaining the difficult situation. The negotiation has been concluded, with the same treatment for both storefronts and residential houses. Renshun Lane is said to be the first to reduce rent through Wuhe.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Issues a Notice to Effectively Carry Out Factory Inspections, and Factories Whose Equipment Is Not Perfected Should Be Inspected According to Law 129

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce issued a notice to the provincial and municipal governments yesterday for the sake of ensuring the safety of workers, stating that not long ago, an explosion occurred at the Shanghai Taiyi Malt Flour Factory, killing and injuring many employees. An Appeal from the Ramie Cloth Industry Association 131

Submitting to Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan

Negotiate with Japan to Cancel Heavy Taxes

Xin Shouheng, Liu Wenliang, Xu Chengqing and other standing committee members of the Jiangxi Ramie Cloth Industry Association in Shanghai submitted a document to Premier Wang, stating that it was submitted for heavy taxes and harsh laws, which are beneficial but not mutual. It is hoped that the matter will be negotiated reasonably to maintain national credibility and sympathize with the difficulties of merchants. China's ramie cloth has been sold in Korea for many years. In the past, Jiangxi Province alone exported about 4 million pieces. After 1927, Japan repeatedly increased tax rates, causing commercial people to suffer losses and slump. According to recent statistics, exports, including Sichuan Province, are only 1 million yuan. The impact is very clear. Now, for coarse ramie cloth, which used to be taxed at 18 yuan or 21 yuan per 100 jin, it has now increased to 32.4 yuan to 45.9 yuan. For fine cloth, which used to be taxed at 32 yuan or 40 yuan, it has now increased to 70.2 yuan to 97.2 yuan. It is estimated that the value is almost equal to 100% of the value. Coarse and fine cloths are also divided into four types: coarse, slightly coarse, top fine, and slightly fine. The taxes are heavy and the laws are harsh. In 1933, the reciprocal agreement signed between China and Japan expired. The association believes that the annual excess of Japanese goods imported is no less than tens of millions. If import taxes on Japanese goods can be slightly increased from then on, it will be for the overall benefit of the country. Even if the ramie cloth item is sacrificed, it will be enough to compensate for the loss. Therefore, even though it is under heavy tax pressure, it has been silently endured without wanting to disturb you. Now, China's newly revised import tariff has been promulgated on July 1. According to a report on July 14, Finance Minister Kong said that although the government has reduced part of the tax rate on Japanese imports, it was originally for the sake of seeking reciprocity. For example, ramie cloth is subject to high taxes, and this is the only way to demand a reduction. Our government pays attention to ramie cloth and has comprehensive plans, not hesitating to sacrifice significant income in order to exchange for reciprocity. The great intention of benefiting industry and commerce and promoting national goods is not only appreciated by hundreds of thousands of industrial and commercial people in the ramie cloth industry, but also celebrated by all citizens. However, since July, Japanese imports have enjoyed the benefits of tax cuts, while China's exports of ramie cloth are still subject to high taxes. Although it is said to be a negotiation, it still takes time. However, it has been several months since then, and there has been no indication from the Japanese government. The association believes that the Japanese are cunning and disregard national credibility. After hesitation, it is difficult to remain silent, so it is submitted to ask you to negotiate strictly, urging them to immediately cancel the heavy taxes on ramie cloth and issue new tax reduction rules so that the country's credibility is consistent with reciprocity in name and reality. As for how much to reduce, the association believes that it can restore the tax rate before 1927 or tax it at the same rate as cotton cloth imports, so that the nearly extinct export of ramie cloth can be hoped to turn around, and the annual import loss can be slightly compensated. Is it appropriate? I beg you to examine and approve, and I am extremely anxious to await orders. Sincerely submit to Wang, President of the Executive Yuan.

The Government of the Dutch East Indies Restricts the Import of Japanese Ceramic Products 132

Because Japanese Merchants Have the Ambition to Monopolize the Market

Therefore, the Regulations on the Import of Ceramics Are Now Promulgated

Chinese Ceramic Merchants Should Take the Opportunity to Work Hard to Promote Sales

According to the International Trade Bureau's Guidance Office, in April of this year, Japanese ceramic importers in Java established the Java Ceramic Importers Association in Surabaya to control the import trade of ceramics in the Dutch East Indies. The Dutch East Indies government believes that this move by Japanese merchants clearly has the ambition to monopolize the market, so on July 25 of this year, it promulgated the Regulations on the Import of Ceramics to restrict it.

China's Exports to the Dutch East Indies 133

There are not many Chinese engaged in the ceramic business in the Dutch East Indies, and the situation is getting worse. According to the Customs Report compiled and published by the Statistics Bureau of the Dutch East Indies, in 1928 and 1929, the total value of China's ports and Hong Kong's annual imports to the Dutch East Indies was about 140,000 guilders. In 1930, it decreased to 126,000 guilders. In 1931, it continued to decrease, with a total of 98,000 guilders. In 1932, it was only 52,000 guilders. European and American products have also not been imported in large quantities in recent years due to the impact of the economic downturn and high costs. Therefore, Japanese goods are the most common household ceramic products in the Dutch East Indies.

Restricting the Import of Japanese Goods 134

Now that the government of the Dutch East Indies has regulations to restrict the import of Japanese goods, all Chinese ceramic merchants should take this opportunity to work hard to promote sales in order to develop. It is hoped that domestic ceramic merchants will pay close attention to it. The restriction regulations were promulgated on July 25 and came into effect on the 26th, with a validity period of three months. The full text of the regulations has a total of 13 articles, and its main points are approximately as follows:

Import Quantity Regulations 135

During the three-month period of validity of the regulations, except for those ordered to be imported by the Dutch East Indies government, the ceramics and their quantities that are allowed to be imported are as follows: (1) Statistics number, from 423 to 435 (coarse ceramics from item A to item G) 53,000 dozen; (2) Statistics number 436 (other coarse ceramics) 325,000 dozen; (3) Statistics number from 437 to 445 (fine ceramics from item a to item f) 1,175,000 dozen; (4) Statistics number 444 and 446 (fine ceramics from 7 to item g) 785,000 kg; (5) Statistics number 447 (ceramic tableware and refined luxury goods) 408,000 kg.

Distribution of Import Quantity 136

The distribution of the import quantity in the preceding paragraph is divided into the following three groups: (1) Importers who are within the territory of the Dutch East Indies, have been approved by the Minister of Economy, and have joined the European Chamber of Commerce for at least four months before January 1, 1934, or have been recognized by the Minister of Economy as similar organizations, such as the Batavia Importers Association and the Hantang Colonial Exporters Association, may have their import quantity determined by the Minister of Economy, accounting for 60% of the total quantity in the preceding paragraph; (2) Importers who do not fall under the provisions of the preceding paragraph may have their import quantity determined by the Minister of Economy, accounting for 40% of the total quantity in the preceding paragraph; (3) If the quantity of the previous 60% is not full, the Minister of Economy may add the remaining quantity to the 40% of importers, or keep it for issuing special permits.

Application for Import Procedures 137

From the date of implementation of these regulations, those who intend to import the ceramics listed in the preceding paragraph must have a permit issued by the Minister of Economy or in the name of the Minister. The permit shall be issued by the applicant signing a request form, and should state the quantity of each type of ceramic to be imported and the quantity of each type of goods imported by the applicant in 1933.

Import Quantity Standard 138

The standard for the distribution of import quantity, regarding the importers who account for 60% of the total quantity, should be determined by the Minister of Economy in proportion to their benefits, consulting the opinion of the five-member committee appointed by the board of directors of the Batavia Importers Association. The quantity obtained by the importers who account for 40% of the total quantity is proportional to the quantity of such goods they imported in 1933, but shall not exceed one-quarter of the quantity of such goods they imported in that year.

The Taxpayers Association Asks the Municipal Council to Pay Attention to Two Points 139

1. Changing the Amount of Rent is Actually Increasing the Donation

2. If Tax Revenue Decreases, the Vacant House Donation Should Be Reported Immediately

The Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession, based on Chen Tingrui's lawyer representing the Great China Hotel and others, requested that the Donations Office of the Municipal Council increase the estimated amount, and sent letters to the Municipal Council and replied to Lawyer Chen as follows:

Letter to the Municipal Council 140

Gentlemen, According to a letter from lawyer Chen Tingrui, "According to the managers of our clients, the Great China Hotel, Oriental Hotel, Huizhong Hotel, Wugong Hotel, Juelu Hotel, New World Hotel, and Great Shanghai Hotel, they recently received letters from the Donations Office of the Municipal Council, and the rent of all our establishments was re-estimated according to the Donations Office's own free will, in order to be the standard for the actual 14% general donation. For example, the original rent of the Great China Hotel was 31,888 yuan, and the increased rent was 48,000 yuan, an increase of more than 50%. The original rent of the Oriental Hotel was 50,400 yuan, and the increased rent was 74,400 yuan, an increase of slightly less than 48%. The original rent of the Huizhong Hotel was 36,502 yuan, and the increased rent was 56,700 yuan, an increase of 62%. The original rent of the Wugong Hotel was 16,782 yuan, and the increased rent was 20,160 yuan, an increase of 20%. The original rent of the Juelu Hotel was 16,782 yuan, and the increased rent was 22,380 yuan, an increase of 33%. The original rent of the Great Shanghai Hotel was 33,566 yuan, and the increased rent was 42,482 yuan, an increase of 27%. As for the New World Hotel, although a part of the lower-level city room has been returned and the rent has been reduced to 1,600 yuan per month, the Donations Office must insist on calculating the annual rent as 27,000 yuan. Although our hotels and the acting lawyer have repeatedly negotiated and protested, it has been ineffective. Moreover, the Municipal Council recently sent a letter limiting our hotels to appeal to the Municipal Council's own valuation committee within two weeks, otherwise it will be considered tacit consent. Therefore, we request your lawyer to fight the Municipal Council legally again, etc." Having been entrusted by our lawyer, after thinking again and again, we believe that this matter is of great importance, not only involving the interests of a few of our clients, but also related to the interests of all residents of the Public Concession. We believe that your association is the only representative organization of Chinese taxpayers in the Public Concession. Over the years, as our taxpayers have defended legal rights and advocated justice, it has been obvious to all. The case at hand is of great importance, and your association should also represent our clients and protest to the Municipal Council, asking it to collect general donations according to the rent as usual, and not to overcharge in order to show fairness and protect legal rights. The above has been reported to the association. Now, please pay attention to the following two points: (1) Changing the amount of rent during the taxpayers' meeting and increasing it. Although the donation rate is still 14%, it is actually increasing the donation, making the resolution of the taxpayers' meeting invalid. This is a command to change the law. (2) If the market is declining, there are more vacant houses, and tax revenue is decreasing, the resolution of the general assembly of our association to collect general donations on vacant houses should be implemented immediately to increase tax revenue. Correspondingly, we ask you to investigate and not allow conflicts between legislation and administration to occur and shake. This is addressed to the General Manager of the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council.

Re-Statement by Lawyer Chen 141

Addressing the matter directly: I have received your letter dated October 13th, concerning the arbitrary overestimation of rents for the Great China Hotel and other properties by the Public Concession Works Department Donation Office, with the intention of illegally increasing donations. You requested that I protest to the bureau and provide answers to two points: (1) Whether the Public Concession Works Department's collection of a 1.4% general donation is based on the residents' rents as a standard, or whether it can be freely estimated by the department; (2) Whether the rent valuation committee established by the Public Concession Works Department has been formally recognized by this association. I have reviewed this carefully.

Upon investigation, the Public Concession Works Department Donation Office's actions, on the one hand, given the daily decline of the market and the increasing number of vacant properties, are due to powerful forces obstructing them from implementing the resolution of this session's representative assembly regarding the collection of general donations on vacant properties. Therefore, they intend to evade the "no increase in donation rate" resolution of the taxpayers' meeting by covertly increasing rents to achieve the reality of increased donations. For example, the Great China Hotel's rent has been increased by over 50%, which is equivalent to increasing the donation rate by half, from 1.4% to 2.1%. Other cases can be deduced similarly.

On the other hand, those in charge disregard the suffering of the public and exhaust resources for personal gain, to demonstrate their ability to collect taxes. In reality, this kind of action is absolutely illegal. Since the taxpayers' meeting has already resolved that the donation rate for this year will not be increased and will remain at 1.4%, the number of all rents, except for landlords increasing rents, newly built houses with newly determined rents, and discovered underreported rents, cannot be changed by the executors. Otherwise, it would be an "order changing the law." This cannot and should not be allowed by the members of a self-governing body known for its rule of law. If it is not vigorously corrected and allowed, then even if the donation rate is not increased, the standard (rent) number will be increased, and the taxpayers' total donation burden will have increased. The taxpayers' resolution will have been used to cover up the situation. What power will they have to stop the executors from increasing the taxpayers' burden and to form a politically balanced stalemate with the executors?

The implications of this case are not just about the few companies like the Great China Hotel, nor just about the hotel industry, but about all taxpayers. Moreover, in the view of this association, it is shaking the very foundation of the rule of law within this concession. The seriousness of the situation is beyond what those who specialize in collecting taxes can comprehend. Therefore, this association will continue to protest.

Regarding whether the Public Concession Works Department's collection of a 1.4% general donation is based on rent as a standard or can be freely estimated, although the regulations of the Yangjingbang Real Estate Charter belong to the latter, the real estate situation in this concession was different when that charter was created. It was mostly self-built for personal use. Given the circumstances at the time, it could not be otherwise. Later, "rental housing" emerged, and rents were still estimated, but always below the actual rent, just as current real estate valuations are below market prices. This article, which was a good method for the bureau to encourage or cultivate tax sources, was originally a policy and not very consistent with the principles of taxation. Later, donations were collected based on actual rents, so tax collectors had the practice of verifying rent receipts, and landlords had the responsibility to report rent amounts. Those who falsely reported rent amounts were penalized by the court (see page 16, line 5 of this association's important documents from the 22nd year of the Republic of China). Otherwise, these actions would be like child's play. As for self-produced and self-used houses, which originally had no rent amount, they inevitably had to be estimated, but the number should be based on the number at the time the taxpayers' meeting decided on the donation rate and should never be changed afterwards. Moreover, it must be based on land prices and commodity prices as a standard. However, land prices and commodity prices in Shanghai are trending downwards, so even if changes are desired, they should only be reductions. Moreover, these changes must be decided by the taxpayers' meeting. If executors can change them freely, then what need is there for a taxpayers' meeting?

Regarding the organization of the Public Concession Works Department's rent valuation committee, it is an affiliated agency of the Public Concession Works Department and has no legal basis, whether written or unwritten. This association has not recognized it. I am corresponding to reply, hoping you will look into it. This is addressed to Lawyer Chen Tingrui.

Chairman Chiang Orders Military Police to Protect the Jiangxi Provincial Capital National Exhibition 142

The October Issue of Shen Bao Monthly is Published 144

The October issue of Shen Bao Monthly was published on the 15th. The materials in this issue are extremely rich and contain in-depth discussions of recent major international events, such as "The International Situation After the Soviet Union's Entry into the League," "The Kansai Wind Disaster in Japan," "Some Observations on the Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway," and "China and This Year's League of Nations Assembly." These articles can enable readers to understand the developments in the international situation. Regarding domestic politics and finance, there are three articles: "Ways to Solve the Tibetan Question," "On Managing Exchange Rate Policies," and "A Critique of China's Protest Against the U.S. Silver Policy," which contain many unique insights. In addition, "British Military Deployment in the Near East," "The Recent Struggle Between the Democratic and Republican Parties in the United States (American Correspondence)," and "Poland and the Issue of European Minorities" offer detailed analyses and are worthy of reference. This issue contains two local correspondence articles, one titled "Overview of the Baiyi Ethnic Group in Yunnan," which describes the unique customs and folk customs of the Baiyi and is quite interesting, and one titled "The Truth About the Yunnan Ban Hong Issue," which contains rare materials and can be considered a special feature. At present, rural construction and production education are attracting much attention. This issue of Shen Bao Monthly also contains articles such as "Where is the Road to Rural Construction in China?" and "Revisiting the Issue of Education and Production in China," which are also timely works. The literary section, such as random thoughts and novels, has more content than before. Those who like to read literary works should also read this issue of the monthly magazine.

Unidentified Male Corpse Near Jiangwan: Head Crushed into Two Halves 145

The night before last, the 15th, a train passing through the railway tracks near Jiangwan crushed and killed an unidentified man, about 30 years old. His head was crushed into two halves, and the blood and flesh were blurred, a terrible sight. After receiving the report, the court dispatched prosecutor Yang An, along with examiner Xuan Zhiming, to the scene. City Detective Team Uncovers Human Trafficking in Chongming: Lu A'shi Confesses Without Hesitation 146

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Detective Team, on the morning of the day before yesterday at 11 a.m., suddenly received a tip that many babies had recently arrived at the residence of Lu A'bao, located at No. 1, Lane 20, Xundao Street, Nanshi Dadongmen, crying all day long, which was suspicious. The team immediately dispatched foreman Chen Guangyan to supervise detective Zhang Yanbiao, together with police chief Wang Shaofeng of the Xundao Street Police Station, to go to the address and search. As a result, five unidentified male and female babies were found in Lu's home. Lu was immediately arrested, along with his wife, Bao (43 years old), and the suspect Shi Lu (36 years old), and taken back to the team. When Captain Lu proposed to conclude the interrogation, according to Lu A'bao's confession, he was 44 years old, from Chongming, and made a living by selling mutton. All five babies were purchased cheaply from poor families in his hometown and brought to Shanghai with the intention of selling them. As the matter concerned human trafficking, an official document was immediately prepared to submit the case to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. The five babies were sent to the Puyutang orphanage for care.

Old Man Cuts Open Abdomen in Suicide 149

Widowed Daughter-in-Law's Unsuccessful Admonishment

Intestines Flow Out, Life Hangs by a Thread

Xia Lifafa, 56 years old, a local farmer residing at No. 260, Panjiawan, Tanziwan, Zhabei, has a widowed daughter-in-law, Chen, who is now 41 years old. Chen has three daughters, the eldest being 16 years old. Usually, the family lives by Chen's work outside. Recently, Xia Lifafa learned that Chen was having an affair with Jin Guichen, a 48-year-old vegetable vendor living next door. Feeling that it was a disgrace to the family, he often quarreled with his daughter-in-law and Jin Guichen. The day before yesterday, after being slightly humiliated by Jin, Xia Lifafa suddenly had suicidal thoughts. He took a kitchen knife and sneaked into Jin's house while Jin was not home, slashing him in the waist. Jin immediately fell to the ground in a pool of blood with his abdomen cut open and his intestines flowing out. At that time, Xia Chen was out picking wool. Only Xia Lifafa's granddaughters were at home. After learning about it, they cried and reported to the nearby Tanziwan Police Station, which dispatched officer Liu Jianchen to the scene and sent the injured man to the Second Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Hospital for treatment. Due to the severity of the injuries, his life was hanging by a thread. The police station then summoned Xia's daughter-in-law Chen and her lover Jin Guichen to the case and submitted it to the Xinzha Branch Bureau for transfer to the Public Security Bureau for disposal.
