Baking Flatbread Leads to Bloody Incident 151

Both Sides Eager for Private Fighting

A Ningbo native, nicknamed Tang Beef, who was a fishmonger residing on the mezzanine floor of No. 20, Fuxing Lane, East Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, went to a flatbread stall at No. 48, Lane Entrance at 1 a.m. yesterday because he was hungry. He used three copper coins to buy baked buns to fill his stomach and asked the stall owner to reheat the buns in the oven, but the stall owner refused, leading to a quarrel. The stall owner and his shop assistants (all from Shandong) beat Tang Beef. Tang, being outnumbered, returned home and, together with his roommate, a Ningbo native nicknamed Rotten Sand Yuan, went to argue and reprimand the flatbread stall owner. People persuaded them to return. Unexpectedly, the flatbread stall owner gathered more than ten fellow villagers, each holding iron rulers and bayonets, and rushed to No. 20, Fuxing Lane, to provoke Tang Beef, beating anyone they encountered. They slashed and injured Yang Sheng, the son of the second landlord of the building, in the head. The heads of Tang Beef and Rotten Sand Yuan were both broken by the Shandong people with iron rulers, and blood flowed all over their faces. The stall owner and others, seeing that their goal had been achieved, dispersed in a rush. Later, the patrolling police arrived and took the three injured people to the police station for treatment and then sent detectives to the flatbread stall and arrested the stall owner and three shop assistants for investigation.

Patriotic Martyr Pan Hongsheng Released from Prison on Bail Yesterday Morning 153

Immediately Sent to a Doctor for Treatment in the Afternoon

Various Circles Set to Meet on the 18th to Discuss Assistance

According to Xinxin She, the patriotic martyr Pan Hongsheng, suffering from tuberculosis, had his family member Pan Shi apply for bail for medical treatment, which was approved by the Second Branch of the High Court. Pan Shi, along with acting lawyer Ma Junshuo, went to the Tilanqiao Prison yesterday morning to provide bail and lead him out of prison for medical treatment. The details are as follows:

(Arrest Details) Pan Hongsheng, 22 years old, from Suzhou, was a student in a paper shop. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, he participated in the Blood Soul Elimination Traitor Group (also known as the National Soul Elimination Traitor Group) with Liu Chongwu, Tian Shuiyang, and others, hoping to warn奸商 merchants who sell enemy goods. He threw bombs or gave warnings to Sun Guangxing Clock Shop, Mao Tai Xin Foreign Goods Shop, and other places. Later, on November 28th, Liu Chongwu was arrested, leading to the arrest of Pan Hongsheng, Tian Shuiyang, and others. They were subsequently sentenced to twelve years in prison by the court. Later, after lawyer Ma Junshuo appealed on their behalf, the Second Branch of the High Court changed the sentence to six years.

(Release Details) At 9 a.m. yesterday, Pan Shi, accompanied by lawyer Ma Junshuo and Chen Binghui and Chen Jiufeng from the Patriotic Martyr Support Association, went to Tilanqiao Prison to meet Warden Wanant. After explaining the reasons, the warden ordered the prison guard to bring out inmate No. 1654 (Pan Hongsheng), verified his identity, and, after Chen Binghui provided surety, led him out of prison. They rode in cars to Lawyer Ma's office for a brief rest. In the afternoon, Pan Shi accompanied him to Dr. Yu Yunxiu's clinic for treatment. It is reported that his condition is quite serious and it is planned to send him to the Red Cross for treatment this morning.

(Serious Illness) Yesterday afternoon, a reporter from Xinxin She went to Lawyer Ma's office to inquire and happened to meet Pan Hongsheng. He was wearing a dark blue padded shirt and plain colored cloth shoes. His head was shaved, his eyes were dull, his face was haggard, like white paper, and he was in low spirits. His voice was weak and feeble when talking. He was skinny as a rake. It was clear at a glance that he was suffering from severe tuberculosis. The reporter briefly inquired about the situation in prison, saw that he could not talk much, and left.

(Assistance from All Circles) Chen Binghui and others from the Patriotic Martyr Support Association believed that after the release of the young man Pan Hongsheng on bail, he would need to recuperate immediately. However, his situation was very difficult. His parents were old and would have to do everything possible to raise money for their son's treatment. Therefore, they specifically planned to convene the Patriotic Martyr Support Association at 2 p.m. on the 18th of this month to discuss assistance methods for recuperation.

A Tumor the Size of a Football Grows on the Bladder Membrane 155

Weighing Thirty Pounds

Tu Changsheng's Strange Disease

Tu Changsheng, residing at No. 3, Dingjia Lane, West Baoxing Road, Zhabei, originally had a hernia. Last summer, a tumor suddenly grew next to his bladder membrane, initially the size of a citron. Although he felt swollen, he did not pay much attention to it. Over time, it grew larger and larger, and his crotch became burdensome, as if a ball was hanging. He staggered when he walked, which was very painful for Tu. He had no choice but to use a large piece of cloth to bag the tumor and tie it around his neck, barely able to walk, suffering greatly. Recently, unable to bear it any longer, he sought treatment at the Shanghai Sanatorium, run by the Seventh-day Adventist Church in Shenjiawan. After examination by Dr. Bu Mingde, he was deemed to be treatable with surgery. The surgery was performed yesterday afternoon, and the fleshy tumor, as large as a football, was separated from Tu. When placed in a container, it weighed no less than thirty pounds. It was truly a strange disease. According to our reporter, this type of disease is rare. The cause of the disease is not just one, but eating unclean pork and greasy oil are major causes of the disease. Fortunately, the patient resolutely ordered the doctor to remove it, not only eliminating the tumor of more than a year at once, but also liberating himself. The tumor has now been preserved by the sanatorium for medical research, which will greatly contribute to the exploration of the cause of the disease.

Two Escaped Prisoners Prosecuted 156

The Two Prisoners Admit Attempting to Escape Unsuccessfully

Zhang Huicai, Zhao Yunzu, Liu Agui, and other three prisoners serving sentences for theft in the Jiangsu Second Special District Prison on Xuehuali Road, French Concession, colluded to tear cloth into strips and twist them into ropes to escape. At about 3 a.m. on September 5th, just as the prisoners were being unlocked to go to the meal room to receive their meals, Zhang and Zhao ordered Liu to climb the wall using the rope to escape. However, Liu lost his footing due to panic and fell from a high place, injuring his head. The guards discovered this and put Zhang and Zhao in heavy shackles and placed them in separate rooms. Liu died due to ineffective treatment. Zhang and Zhao were transferred to the prosecutor's office of the Second Special Court for investigation and prosecution. This case has been previously reported. After prosecutor Wang Ren concluded the investigation and several court hearings, he filed a public prosecution based on the crime of attempted escape under the criminal law. At the same court's criminal court, chief judge Wang Gangxu, along with prosecutor Wang, held a criminal hearing in the first court yesterday to interrogate them and summoned prison warden Wang Baochang and guards Xiao Wenyin, Nie Zhenchun, and Fu Maoshun to the case to testify. First, the prosecutor stated the intention of the prosecution. Then, Huang Huicai and Zhao Yunzu were interrogated, and they admitted that they had attempted to escape unsuccessfully. The rest of their confessions were the same as those given in the investigative court. Zhang also presented a piece of paper filled with tiny writing, detailing the abuse and beatings in prison and requesting the court to investigate and redress his grievances. The court verified the confessions and ordered them to be remanded in custody and scheduled another hearing. The two prisoners were still sent to prison for execution.

City Chamber of Commerce Convenes Various Brokerage Industries Yesterday 157

Continued to Hold the Second Joint Meeting

The brokerage industries in this city have submitted petitions to the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting that the brokerage rules and tax collection rules issued by the City Finance Bureau be difficult to implement and request a transfer for improvement. The City Chamber of Commerce convened a joint meeting of various brokerage industries on the 27th of last month and passed six resolutions, which the City Chamber of Commerce sent to the Finance Bureau for adoption. The association received a reply from the Finance Bureau, which extended the verification deadline to October 31 but did not accept the rest. Therefore, it convened a second joint meeting of various brokerage industries at 1 p.m. yesterday. Sun Mingqi and Yuan Hongjun, representatives of the City Chamber of Commerce, Rao Hanzhang, Shao Yunxuan, and Zhang Xilin, representatives of the Chicken and Duck Industry Association, Fei Tinghua of the Medicinal Materials Industry, Qiu Liangyu and Yu Zhiqing of the Local Goods Industry, Xin Wenyao of the Pig Industry, Zhu Weinan of the Tree Firewood Industry, Xin Dingsan of the Charcoal Industry, Xue Meiting of the Sugar Industry, Sun Guchen of the Fresh Fish Industry, Shao Baoxing of the Seafood Sundries Industry (Li, proxy), Cai Runshan of the Fruit Local Goods Industry, Zhu Jinwen and Qu Shunshang of the Miscellaneous Firewood Industry, Cai Yikun and Gu Xinyi of the Bean Rice Industry (Zhu, proxy), Ma Jiliang of the Wood Industry, Zhu Shujian of the Liang Shaojiu Industry, Ma Fuxing and Xu Menghua of the Brick Ash Industry, Cheng Youfu of the Flower Industry, and other more than 60 representatives from more than 20 industries attended. Chairman Sun Mingqi first reported on the Finance Bureau's reply and the letters from various industry associations. Then, representatives from the sugar, seafood sundries, and brick ash industries reported that their industries were not acting as agents for buying and selling and were not responsible for profits and losses, which was inconsistent with the brokerage rules set by the Finance Bureau, and requested that the City Chamber of Commerce transfer the request to cancel the brokerage license. After further statements by the representatives about the reasons why limiting commissions was inappropriate and the time was tight, it was resolved to elect representatives based on the resolutions of the previous meeting to reason with the Finance Bureau together with the representatives of the City Chamber of Commerce. The authorities must understand the transaction situation of the local brokerage industry and quickly amend the business rules and tax collection rules. Cai Runshan, Ni Baizhai, Gu Xinyi, Rao Hanzhang, and Xin Wenyao were elected as representatives on the spot. The date will be decided by the City Chamber of Commerce and then notified to the representatives to go together. Other important cases were discussed at the end before the meeting was adjourned.

Having Walked Through Twenty-Nine Countries, Experiencing Immense Hardship

Next Year, He Will Go to Soviet Russia and Return Home via Siberia

Mr. Pan Deming, a young walker, joined the Chinese Youth Asia Walking Group two years ago and set off from Shanghai. At that time, those who joined the group included Ms. Qiu Fang, etc. Later, due to physical reasons, they all withdrew one after another. When they arrived in Annam (Vietnam), only Mr. Pan Deming remained. However, Mr. Pan did not become discouraged by the withdrawal of his comrades. On the contrary, this prompted his ambition to walk around the world. Mr. Huang Jingwan, an educator in this city, recently received a letter from Mr. Pan from the United States, along with many newspaper clippings detailing that Mr. Pan had completed his journey through twenty-nine countries, experiencing immense hardship along the way. His footprints could be found in countries such as England, France, Germany, Italy, Belgium, Switzerland, Annam, India, Yugoslavia, and so on. Foreign newspapers and magazines not only provided detailed accounts of him but also hailed him as a "Chinese Hero." Municipal Health Bureau Plans to Build Kilns to Incinerate Plague Pigs 161

Due to the large number of plague pigs dying this year, the Livestock Inspection Station of the Wusong Health Bureau, coupled with the fact that there are no rendering plants for dead pigs in Shanghai, has resulted in the daily consignment of plague pigs seized by the health bureaus of Pudong Yangjing, South Shanghai Xuejiabang, West Shanghai, and Zhabei to the Wusong rendering plant by truck. Because the plant receives more than forty pigs from various places every day, it is unable to render them all in time, and those that have become rotten are buried in pits. As a result, a foul odor permeates the surrounding area, and Chinese and Western tourists visiting Songbin (Wusong) hold their noses as they pass by. Tang Chengzong, a member of the Wusong Municipal Committee, submitted a request to the municipal government to relocate the rendering plant for the sake of public health, as detailed in previous newspaper reports. It is now learned that the Health Bureau, recognizing that it is impossible to dispose of these rotten plague pigs, has repeatedly consulted on disposal methods but has not yet found a satisfactory solution. It is now heard that it has been agreed to imitate the method of incinerating toxic substances by judicial authorities and build two large cement kilns next to the rendering plant to incinerate the plague pigs. The municipal government instructed the Public Works Bureau yesterday to send personnel to Wusong to survey the site for kiln construction, draw up plans, and submit them to the municipal government. Construction will begin as soon as the order is given. If this method is implemented, the relocation of the rendering plant will likely become a pipe dream.

Chen Yingfei and Other Members of the Jinjiang Fritillaria Marketing Cooperative Arrive in Shanghai 162

Make Important Statements

Chen Yingfei, a member of the Jinjiang Fritillaria Marketing Cooperative in Yin County, and Shao Risheng, a representative for auditing accounts, have come to Shanghai to seek support from public opinion on the fritillaria issue. Chen and Shao made the following statements:

(Statement by Chen Yingfei) (1) Farmers' Hopes for Cooperatives: In recent years, the national economy has declined, and cooperatives are the only way to save rural areas. This is well known. Therefore, before the establishment of the fritillaria cooperative, farmers had high expectations. What they hoped for was reasonable promotion of sales channels, expansion of uses, increase in production, improvement in quality, and elimination of manipulation and exploitation by intermediaries to stabilize the rural economy. As for the selling price, they would be satisfied if it could be maintained at 70 to 80 yuan per dan for a long time. However, the fact that the cooperative has entered into an exclusive sales contract with the four pharmaceutical firms to restrict production is not what the members want to hear. (2) Production and Sales Volume in Recent Years: In previous years, the average annual production of fritillaria was about 800,000 jin, and the sales volume was always around 700,000 jin (suddenly reduced to 320,000 jin after the establishment of the cooperative). The price ranged from 60 to 70 yuan to 80 to 90 yuan. This was due to the relationship between good and bad harvests. However, if the price is slightly higher, the sales volume will inevitably decrease. Farmers are well aware of the cause-and-effect relationship between high prices and sluggish sales. Therefore, the current cooperative's policy of drastically raising prices and restricting production is considered by farmers to be a suicidal policy. (3) The Harm of Not Digging Up Fritillaria: Fritillaria reproduces by having mother and child bulbs. When planted this year, one becomes two next year (according to the law, one should be dug up, leaving one for seed). If it is not dug up, two will become four the year after next. The space occupied by fritillaria in the soil cannot be expanded due to the reproduction of fritillaria. As a result, the fritillaria squeeze each other, the volume is reduced, and the juice dries up, which greatly affects the medicinal effect. Therefore, the method of not digging up the soil is an immoral act. (4) High Fritillaria Prices, Members Not Benefiting: After the establishment of the cooperative, although the selling price of fritillaria has soared several times, the members have not benefited. In the past, when farmers freely sold one dan, they could get the full value of one dan immediately for their normal use. Now, the members of the cooperative receive 60 yuan per dan (the same amount as they would get from free sales), which is paid in four installments over a period of one year. The loss is huge as they receive small amounts sporadically on weekdays. (5) Currently, the members of the cooperative account for about three-quarters of all farm households. Some do not want to join. In theory, the cooperative should win the trust of farmers so that those who have not joined will naturally want to join. However, they do not try to do this. Those who want to save rural areas should be heartbroken when they hear this. (6) Unexpected Disaster: I have 4.5 mu of fritillaria fields, and my family is fairly well-off. As the head of the Dunzong Elementary School in the sixth district of Yin County, I have some knowledge. Seeing that the cooperative violated the principles, I could not help but say something unpleasant. As a result, I was resented by others. On May 20, I was falsely accused of privately digging up fritillaria. My three houses were torn down, and my documents, clothes, and utensils were burned. The mulberry and bamboo trees were cut down, and my 4.5 mu of fritillaria fields were completely destroyed. My wife and I were seriously injured. Although the local court sentenced Cui Qian to one year of imprisonment and Zhou Niangzi to three years, the civil part has not yet been settled. My family is broken and injured, and we have no food or shelter. My parents and wife are always sad. (7) Members Have Completely Lost Faith in the Directors: The members' faith in the directors of the cooperative has been completely lost. The resolution not to dig up the soil has already been completely destroyed. Therefore, they had to convene an extraordinary general meeting of representatives on October 3 to resolve to allow digging up the soil. (8) Omitted.

According to Chen Xunru, the manager of the bank, in recent years, China's economy has declined, and an atmosphere of depression has enveloped society. Commerce has withered and industries have failed everywhere, presenting a situation of collapse. This is an undeniable fact. The reason for this is none other than the lack of economic circulation. Our bank has been preparing for several months and has been officially opened today. In the future, we will serve society faithfully, take the adjustment of the market finance as our responsibility, and hope to use the power of the bank to help the development of industry and promote the revival of society.

Tai Shuangqiu and Others Initiate the Construction of Nian'er New Village 170

Materials are Entirely Domestic Goods

To Suit the Living of the Middle and Lower Classes

Recently, the trend of building new villages has been prevalent in Shanghai. However, most of the buildings are Europeanized and full of extravagance, which are definitely not suitable for ordinary people to live in. Moreover, most of the materials are imported, so that more new villages are built, the more money flows out. This is very noteworthy. Now, Tai Shuangqiu, Tang Maohuai, Wang Jinyi, and other members of the Nian'er Society in West Shanghai have taken this into consideration and gathered more than a dozen comrades to choose a site near Fanwangdu Zhongshan Road to build the Nian'er New Village. The Nian'er Society has always advocated domestic goods, practiced social economy, and improved the lives of the people. The construction of the Nian'er New Village is based on these basic conditions. It is now actively underway.

Recent News on the Dispute Over the Demolition of Houses in Leyi Lane, French Concession 172

Court Prohibits Demolition...Tenants Hold Meeting to Discuss

The houses in Leyi Lane on Annakin Road in the French Concession, due to the owner Jiang Hanzhai filing a lawsuit to rebuild the houses, have aroused the opposition of all the tenants. The tenants have hired lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Zhu Dianqing as representatives to file a petition with the Second Special District Local Court, requesting a ban on demolition and water shutoff, and setting up fences. The court, after receiving the petition, ordered Judge Huang Meiqing to summon the tenant representatives to court. After several interrogations, the court ruled the day before yesterday that the temporary ban on demolition, water shutoff, and setting up fences was approved, and the ruling was sent to both parties yesterday for compliance. It is also heard that the Leyi Lane branch of the Fourth Sub-district Federation of the Shanghai Second Special District held a general meeting at Yanxin Temple on Blair Road at 8:00 p.m. yesterday. All the tenants attended, with Wang Dekui presiding and Yu Jingqing recording. After the report was completed, the following methods were decided for proceeding: (1) All rent arrears from August to November of this year, a total of four months' rent, will be deposited with the Shanghai Bank at Baxianqiao for safekeeping; (2) The deposit method is that it can only be withdrawn with the joint seals of this association; (3) The deposit will be made on November 1 by this association, and thereafter, it will be paid on a monthly basis to facilitate negotiation; (4) A notice will be issued to the three tenants that rent arrears are not allowed; (5) Regarding negotiation expenses, another 3 yuan will be paid for each building. If this is not enough, it will be discussed again; (6) The owner has not yet restored the water supply. A warning letter will be sent immediately to restore it. Otherwise, a decision will be made to file a lawsuit according to law and demand compensation for damages. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Therefore, in the past, silk exports often accounted for a very important position in China's foreign trade. Now, in order to build up children's love for domestic silk and satin, the bureau has decided to hold a donation of children's clothing fabrics from the 18th. Letter to the Editor 185

To the Esteemed Editor:

We are deeply grateful for your newspaper's repeated exposure of the hardships faced by the unfortunate refugees who have been unreasonably expelled by the Japanese government. Your reports have aroused sympathy from all walks of life. However, we have found a news item in yesterday's newspaper stating that three refugees, including Jin Zuo-tou, arrived in Shanghai on the Ikoma Maru at 3:00 PM yesterday (the 15th), which is completely inconsistent with the facts. According to our information, the three refugees, including Jin Zuo-tou, arrived in Shanghai on the Ikoma Maru at 3:00 PM on the 14th. At that time, no newspapers published it. Unexpectedly, yesterday's report mistakenly attributed the arrival of the three refugees on the 14th to the 15th, which is inaccurate. This matter concerns the livelihoods of the refugees. Every time refugees are expelled back to Shanghai, it must be recorded in the register for reporting to the central government to request relief. If the dates are inconsistent, it will not match the reporting date of the expelled refugees and will hinder relief efforts. Therefore, we are sending this letter to correct the information and would be grateful if you could publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column.

Sincerely,

Representatives of the Committee of Expelled Overseas Chinese from Japan

Chen Xian-geng, Tian Zuo-lan, 16th.

Special Article

Awakening to National Self-Reliance and Revival (4) 187

— Manuscript by Zhang Yuanruo

At the China Vocational Education Society

9. The Awakening of Youth to National Self-Reliance and Salvation: The position and responsibility of Chinese youth today are even greater than those of the general public. Several years ago, I wrote an article calling on the youth of the country to awaken, earnestly hoping that the youth would awaken. Youth are the new life of our nation's future, so the position of youth is particularly important. The mission that youth bear for the nation is also particularly significant. To save the country, youth must first have the awareness to save the country. To be self-reliant, youth must first have the determination to be self-reliant. Otherwise, there is absolutely no hope for the future of the nation. Therefore, we can be disappointed in everything, but we must not be disappointed in youth. However, there are many undeniable illnesses in the youth of today. However, the creation of these illnesses cannot be entirely blamed on the youth. There are many reasons. Analytically speaking, there are four: (1) Historical: Subject to the inertia of Chinese society for thousands of years, decadent and following old ways, not knowing how to invigorate. The decadence of the Six Dynasties is now prevalent in youth academic circles, causing general promising youth to indulge in the pleasures of sensual delights, and unable to extricate themselves. (2) Of the Times: Modern free thought dominates the psychology of ordinary people. The Chinese, misunderstanding freedom, are increasingly becoming unrestrained. When students take major exams, they hope that the teachers will provide the questions, and the narrower the scope, the better. In the past, teachers controlled students, but now students control teachers. It is truly heartbreaking. The spirit of teachers and academic atmosphere must be rectified. (3) Subjective: The youth themselves are indecisive and do not know how to work hard and love themselves, and therefore willingly degenerate. (4) Objective: There are many youths who, although they are willing to work hard, are discouraged by the darkness of politics and society, and therefore there are many who are passive. There are also a small number of political dignitaries and professors who use students as tools, making them unknowingly become increasingly corrupt. This can be regarded as the greatest sin against youth. Our analysis of the illnesses of youth is not to criticize youth, but to indicate the direction of awakening to youth. Although everything now is heartbreaking and disappointing, the future of the nation completely depends on whether the youth of China today can have the determination to thoroughly renew themselves, be self-aware, and be self-reliant. I feel that a youth occupies a particularly important position in the entire national life, so youth should be the first to have the awareness of self-reliance and salvation. The life of youth is the life of the nation's future. The awakening of youth is the awakening of the nation. The progress of youth is the progress of the nation. Conversely, the degeneration of youth is the degeneration of the nation. The decline of youth is also the decline of the nation. You all must hope that our nation can be revived, then you must make the determination to be self-reliant and save the country from today onwards. Do not be pessimistic, do not reduce the courage to work hard because of the current poor state of the nation. It is precisely because the national situation is critical that there is a need to work hard and struggle. Moreover, the affairs of the world are governed by a certain law of cause and effect. Whatever effort is made, there will be a corresponding harvest. A point of effort will have a point of effect. In the past thousands of years, especially in the past hundred years, we have formed the decline of the nation and created today's serious national crisis because we did not know how to work hard and did not know how to catch up. The meaning of life is to constantly strive upwards. The survival of a nation is the continuation of the total hard work of the people. The life of a nation is not due to birth, and the development and strength of a nation cannot be expected in a day or two, but the result of the continuous and permanent efforts of all the people, regardless of gender, age, occupation. In the eighteenth century, Rousseau (J.J. Rousseau) spoke of liberalism, saying, "The will of every person together becomes public opinion." This is the theoretical basis of his democracy. I am speaking of nationalism, so I do not advocate liberalism, but advocate self-reliance. The effort of every citizen combined becomes "national strength." "National strength" is the foundation of national life, but national strength originates from self-reliance and is based on self-reliance, so I want to promote self-reliance to consolidate the foundation of nationalism, to attempt the revival of the nation, and to use self-reliance to revise Rousseau's liberalism. The eighteenth century could produce the famous Rousseau, but the twentieth century, especially China today, is not an era of liberalism, but an era of self-reliance. To save the country, the first priority is self-awareness and self-reliance. Do not learn the superficialities of others. Moreover, liberalism has now failed. There are thousands of ways to save the country, but the fundamental principle is self-reliance. National strength is made up of self-reliance. With national strength, the national fortune can be saved and the nation can be revived. This is not only a natural conclusion in theory, but also an inevitable result in fact. I hope that you will keep this in mind, act promptly, set an example, and turn words into action. Contribute your intelligence and talents to the country, and place the responsibility of saving the country and reviving the nation on yourselves separately. In this way, every citizen can generate the strength of every citizen, and the combined strength of 400 million people in the country will definitely generate unparalleled national strength that can recreate the life of the Chinese nation and restore the inherent glory of our Chinese nation. Zhu Zhongzheng, stenographer, September 15, 1934

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Heaven 188

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Pitying the Drifting Girl Peeks Through the Door, Wishing to Hear of Hardships, Cherishing Jade Visits a Poor Family

But he didn't dare to walk under the corridor, and stayed far away from Cheng Zhiqian to avoid a direct conflict. Instead, he took a winding path through the center of the courtyard. When Cheng Zhiqian saw her, he couldn't help but feel a stir in his heart. He seemed to have seen this girl somewhere before. Although she didn't shed the appearance of a country girl, she was still clean and tidy, and looked like the daughter of a decent family. He couldn't help but put aside his intention to visit the white man, and focused his attention on this girl. The small-footed woman had already walked up to him, and supported his shoulder, saying: It doesn't matter, I'm very familiar with this place, I come here two or three times almost every day. Most of the teachers here are acquaintances. As she spoke, she walked to the door of Zhang Jiefu's room. The tea boy had already rushed into the room, propped up the door curtain, and nodded with a smile, saying: You don't believe there is an iron bed, come in and take a look. The girl poked her head in and looked, seemingly knowing that there was someone inside, so she said to the small-footed woman: Let's just take a look from outside. The small-footed woman patted her shoulder lightly, saying: You child, you really have no ambition. When you heard it was nice to look at, you wanted to come and see. Now that you're here, you don't want to go in. What are you afraid of with me here? After saying this, she took the girl's hand and went into the room. Cheng Zhiqian suddenly realized that this was Li Shilian, the refugee girl that Li Shilian had mentioned yesterday. He had met this girl on the ferry in Xianyang, so he remembered that her face looked familiar. Since she was a refugee girl, he shouldn't scheme against her, and couldn't help but walk over to see what they were doing, with a bit of a monitoring flavor. As he thought this, Li Shilian also came out of the room. Zhang Jiefu asked a question in the room, "Is this girl also surnamed Hu?" Then he said: "Mr. Li, Mr. Cheng, please come in and sit, I have a visitor here." The girl felt embarrassed in the room, and when she saw two more people outside the window, she pulled the small-footed woman out. Li Shilian smiled and nodded to him, saying: "I also live here, won't you sit for a while?" (41)

Shaoxing Ballads 189

— Nineteen

Anyone who has been to Shaoxing has probably heard of the so-called "Three-Piece Ballads" or seen signs reading "So-and-So's Three-Piece Ballads" hanging one after another near Guanzhu Bridge and Tazi Bridge. The singers of the ballads are all blind people, and they sing together as men and women. The instruments they use are the sanxian, erhu, and yangqin, so they are called "Three-Piece." There are also "Five-Piece" versions, which add an additional erhu and a pipa to the "Three-Piece" ensemble. Among the instruments, the sanxian is the most important. This is similar to the drum and clapper in Peking opera, which are all played by blind men.

When people have celebrations or other events, they often call them to play and sing to liven things up. The price for a performance is said to range from three to five yuan, depending on the generosity of the family celebrating. When those blind people are hired, they actually change into a set of silk clothes, put on a pair of black glasses, and grope their way through the market, which is quite amusing to see. But rather than saying it's amusing, it's more pitiful, because their lives are very hard.

The origin of the ballads cannot be verified, but some say they evolved from Pingdiao (level tone). The tunes are mostly靡靡之音 (decadent music). What they sing is, of course, stories about the joys and sorrows of young masters and young ladies. Before singing the main text, they usually sing a pair of short lyrics called "Jie Shi" (connecting poems). This is similar to Suzhou storytellers singing a pair of opening verses first. It is said that learning to sing the ballads is not easy either. If you can sing the line "曾記梨花細雨天" (I remember the pear blossoms on a drizzly day) in tune, the teacher can have a big "生炒脚魚" (fried soft-shelled turtle) feast. So they have a saying: "曾記梨花細雨天, 生炒脚魚要吃大半年" (I remember the pear blossoms on a drizzly day, I'll be eating fried soft-shelled turtle for half a year). As for why they have to use "fried soft-shelled turtle" to thank the teacher, that is not known. The scripts of the ballads are only passed down orally; it is difficult to investigate them; otherwise, they could be used as a great material for studying popular literature.

Tidbits 190

— (Jijue)

The telegraph office has launched social telegrams, charging only three cents per word. Sending a social telegram is like sending an express letter, which is very popular. Therefore, the post office also has a so-called "ordinary express delivery" method, which charges twice as much as ordinary letters, but seven cents less than express letters. The "middle way" will surely be popular!

The Impoverished Scholars of Yangzhou 191

— Wang Shouqiu

Speaking of the impoverished scholars of Yangzhou, I have to say "culture has declined." Originally, these so-called impoverished scholars are a kind of disguised beggar. Although there are many literary beggars in Shanghai who make a living by writing, those literary beggars make a living by selling their writings, and do not really go begging. Only these impoverished scholars of Yangzhou are indeed genuine "literary beggars."

Some of these impoverished scholars have indeed experienced the "ten years of cold window," but unfortunately their fate was not good and they were unable to "achieve fame in one fell swoop." In the past, they could still find a job as a private tutor to make a living, but now, with schools everywhere, who would hire you, a sour scholar of 之乎者也? Therefore, for the sake of making a living, they had to embark on the path of impoverished scholars. The begging locations for the impoverished scholars are teahouses and families with happy events. Therefore, the people of Yangzhou are a little afraid of these impoverished scholars, because if they are not entertained well, and their desires are not satisfied, they often slam the table and make a lot of noise, causing "teapots and teacups to fly together, and benches and tables to dance together," which would not make the guests unhappy? Therefore, they are always treated with all kinds of perfunctory responses, and their arrogance is getting higher and higher!

Among the impoverished scholars, there are indeed many sons of fallen nobles, but most of them are only rudimentarily literate and use the words "impoverished scholar" as a protective charm for begging. We should naturally help those genuine scholars and provide them with a place to live and a way to make a living; however, those fake impoverished scholars should also be banned in order to maintain the dignity of scholars.

Two Unhealthy Mentalities of Our People 192

— (Shiying)

The obsequious mentality towards foreigners in the upper class, the fearful mentality towards foreigners in the lower class

Records of the Fragrant Imperial Carriages 193

— Original by Princess Der Ling, Translated by Qin Shouou

The Empress Dowager suddenly turned her gaze to the east, her face facing Fengtian; she was still muttering to herself intermittently, but because her voice was too low, I couldn't hear clearly what she was saying. Her eyes revealed a strange emotion, as if she had discovered some figures or scenes at a very distant distance, so she was attracted to it; however, none of us had such illusions, we just followed her old self and looked westward randomly.

Finally, the old Buddha had looked enough by herself, and then returned to the car, ordering it to start.

The train, of course, was still moving very slowly, slowly leaving the station like an earthworm, staggering step by step towards the gap in the Great Wall. When our locomotive rolled into the border of the Northeast, we were still lingering within the mainland of China! Then, our yellow train left the Middle Earth one by one and entered our hometown. Although I don't have a deep sense of place, but according to the facts, the Northeast is indeed our hometown that we cannot deny! Our ancestors grew up on this land.

The ancestors of the Old Buddha, the Yehenala clan, are also natives here. The Northeast also created an unparalleled figure for China, who made China's entire history greatly change because of him. That is none other than Nurhaci, the founding emperor of the Qing Dynasty! Later, the emperors of the Qing Dynasty, from Shunzhi, Kangxi, Yongzheng, Qianlong, Jiaqing, Daoguang, Xianfeng (the Empress Dowager's husband)...to Guangxu, were all descendants of Nurhaci. (151)

The Fresh Water Chestnuts of Suzhou 194

— Yao Tianyu

In my hometown of Suzhou, it is now the time when the water chestnuts in the ponds are ripe. The red ones are rouge red, the green ones are emerald green, very bright and very beautiful.

Groups of three to five country girls, twelve or thirteen years old, wearing small shirts of blue cloth with white flowers, rolling up their sleeves high, with bare feet, using bathtubs as boats, pushing bamboo poles, while the boats move slowly, reaching into the heart of the pond, picking and picking. Their mouths are still singing their country songs, the songs are not uniform; but to others, it only feels that their singing is rippling in the autumn sky, exceptionally natural and exceptionally beautiful. Under such a happy mood, they forgot their hardships.

Until the red sun sets in the west, they also sell these abundant harvests to the families by the river. The subtle sounds, with a musical rhythm, are also fascinating. People are attracted by this kind of sound, and they all want to buy some to taste, so the fresh, sweet taste has become widespread among everyone's tongues.

Such things will continue until the season when autumn is deep, the dew is cold, and the grass and trees are yellow.

The water chestnuts here, perhaps, are transported from my hometown? But the quantity does not seem to be much! The water chestnuts in the baskets of the average seller are either scorched yellow or blackened, and the meat inside must have lost its original freshness; except for being able to be taken to make food for small insects like "drop bells," people shouldn't eat them, right? Sometimes they are also mixed with rotten water chestnuts, which is of course even more unacceptable. Therefore, I have never eaten fresh water chestnuts here once.

Little Recipe

Japanese Cuisine (Part 1) 195

— Bingyu

The two characters for "cuisine" mean "dishes." Japanese cuisine refers to the dishes of the Eastern people, the Japanese. Having stayed in Japan for six years, I am quite familiar with the situation there. I usually paid close attention to the country's customs, habits, and diet. During my stay, I would venture out alone every Sunday to observe social conditions. Besides classmates, my friends included the section chief of the court, the compradore of a company, and several teachers in schools. They were willing to travel with me regardless of seniority. The former principals, Dr. Shida and Dr. Yoshino, as well as the scholar of Chinese studies, Ota, were all friends of my teachers. Because I was a self-funded student, my family could provide some financial support from time to time, which was more comfortable than the government-funded students who were limited to seventy yuan a month. Therefore, I didn't care about the slightest expense when spending money. Moreover, most of my friends were from the middle and upper classes. Naturally, I couldn't avoid socializing with them. I have eaten Japanese food so many times in six years that I have lost count. (Most foreign students live in hotels run by Chinese, or in boarding houses run by Japanese with Chinese kitchens, or rent a room with meals provided by the landlord.) The food they eat on weekdays is usually neither fully Chinese nor fully Japanese. Now, I will tell the readers about the dishes that Japanese people eat and how they eat them, because many friends and colleagues have often asked me about it, wanting to try it. I repeatedly told them that if they ate Japanese food, they would definitely vomit for three days, and it would be better to buy a piece of stinky tofu to eat, which would be more flavorful. However, they always didn't believe me. Now, I will write down the names of various dishes so that you can understand. However, some dishes imitate Chinese-style cooking, which are still acceptable. Most of the other strange dishes that are neither Chinese nor Western nor anything in between are frightening to see, nauseating to smell, and make you want to vomit. If you don't believe me, you might as well try it at a Japanese restaurant run by Japanese expatriates in various ports, and then you will believe it. There are many types of Japanese cuisine. Ordinary formal meals include two soups and five dishes, or two soups and seven dishes, or three soups and seven dishes. Generally, families above the middle class use two soups and five dishes. Other informal cuisines and social customs are like in the north and south of our country, which vary according to local customs.

(1) The formal meal of two soups and five dishes. This kind of formal meal can represent the entirety of Japanese cuisine. Various flavors are probably complete. If you go to a restaurant to eat, each meal costs at least five yuan and no more than ten yuan. The order of serving the formal meal is divided into four times. The first time is called "suimono," which means soup. The Japanese call it "shiimono," which is a covered bowl, a basin, and a small plate. There is a bowl of soup inside, which is a mixture of sea bream and wax gourd. There is also "sunomono," which means vinegared dish, which is made of sea bream and seaweed. There is also a basin of "sakana," which means soy-glazed fish, which is sea bream grilled with salt and soy sauce. The second course is called "honzen," which means the main course, which is a covered bowl, a large bowl, and a small plate. There is a bowl of soup inside, which is made of flour, shiitake mushroom pieces, and yam. ) Sashimi (is a kind of bonito slice, red ark shell meat, white radish, seaweed, shiitake mushroom, siler, and shredded ginger served in a large plate) Tsubo dish (is a mixture of large shrimp, lily bulbs, and shredded shiitake mushrooms) Pickles (are raw green vegetables, radishes, pickled ginger, etc.) The third course is three bowls, called "nizen," which is a flat bowl (yellow croaker, shrimp, winter mushrooms, yam, and Japanese honewort mixed and cooked) A small cup (is a mixture of red root yam and grilled shellfish) Soup (cooked with turnip and orchid) The fourth course is a large bowl, called "sanzen" (which is grilled sea bream) The way they eat formal meals is that when they entertain guests at home, they usually use two soups and five dishes, but the cooking methods vary due to different traditions. There are styles that imitate the court's Shijō school, and there are styles that imitate the warrior's Ogasawara school. Even the order of serving the dishes is not fixed. For example, when eating soup, the maid will bring out the wine. (Male servants are not used in Japan.) The authentic Japanese sake is similar to our country's rose dew wine, sweet and fragrant. When serving wine, the maid holds the wine bottle with both hands. At this time, the man uses his left hand and the woman uses her right hand to pick up the cup, and she pours the wine. The first cold sake is called "reishu." After drinking it, there is also "atsukan" (which is hot sake). If you don't drink alcohol, you can't refuse completely. You should pretend to drink a sip or two. After that, if they pour more, you can politely decline.

Education News

Guangdong Schools Teach Classics and Instructions 196

▲ Stipulating teaching time and textbooks

▲ To be implemented from the 23rd academic year

The Guangdong authorities recently promoted the study of classics in schools. The provincial government ordered the provincial Department of Education to handle the matter. After receiving the order, the Department of Education first organized a Classics and Instructions Compilation and Review Committee to compile classics and instructions textbooks for primary and secondary schools. Since then, various identification books have been compiled one after another and handed over to booksellers for printing to catch up with the start of the 23rd academic year so that they can be adopted by primary and secondary schools. The implementation measures for the classics and instructions have also been drafted by the Department of Education and submitted to the 327th Provincial Affairs Conference for approval. The implementation measures for classics and instructions in primary and secondary schools in Guangdong Province are recorded below for your quick review. From the 23rd academic year, senior primary schools and secondary schools at all grades will implement classics and instructions in accordance with the following measures: (1) Time: (A) According to Article 3 of the Standards for Elementary School Curriculum issued by the Ministry, "The total time is moderate and may be increased or decreased by ninety minutes per week depending on local conditions." The classics and instructions time for elementary schools will be increased by ninety minutes per week. (B) Secondary schools at all levels will give lectures on classics and instructions for two hours per week. (2) Books: (A) Senior elementary schools will use the Classic of Filial Piety (annotated by Emperor Xuanzong of Tang) and the Classics and Instructions Reader as textbooks. (1) The eighteen chapters of the Classic of Filial Piety will be read over two years. The first grade of senior primary school will read four chapters each semester, and the second grade of senior primary school will read five chapters each semester. (2) The Classics and Instructions Reader will be one volume per year. (B) Secondary schools will use the Four Books (annotated by Zhu Xi) as textbooks. (1) The twenty chapters of the Analects will be read over three years. The first grade of junior high school will read three chapters each semester, the second grade will read four chapters in the first semester and three chapters in the second semester, and the third grade will read four chapters in the first semester and three chapters in the second semester. (2) The seven chapters of Mencius will be read in the first grade of senior high school, three chapters, and the second grade will read four chapters. (3) The first chapter of the Great Learning and ten chapters of Commentary will be read in the first semester of the third grade of senior high school. (4) The thirty-three chapters of the Doctrine of the Mean will be read in the second semester of the third grade of senior high school. (3) Teachers: Classics and instructions teachers will be hired by the principals of each school and must meet the qualifications of primary and secondary school teachers and have research on classics. (4) Teaching methods: (A) If the original meaning of the classics and instructions is inconsistent with the national system and modern trends, the classics and instructions teachers should explain in detail the relationship between the times, environment, and political system in accordance with the meaning of "adapting to the times" in order to adapt. (B) The implementation of classics and instructions is to instill basic moral knowledge in primary and secondary school students so that they can study and put it into practice. Therefore, attention should be paid to practice in order to achieve the effect of physical practice. (October 12)

Ministry of Education Meeting on Public Education Implementation Measures 197

The Ministry of Education convened a meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 15th to discuss the implementation measures for public education. The meeting was attended by the directors and section chiefs of the competent department (Social Education Department) and supervisors. The meeting was chaired by Vice Minister Duan Xipeng and discussed three major issues: (1) the compilation of textbooks for public schools; (2) the improvement of reading materials for public schools; (3) the promotion of public schools. It was decided that for the first issue (compilation of textbooks for public schools), specific measures should be formulated first so that the compilation can begin. The second issue (improvement of reading materials for public schools) and the third issue (promotion of public schools) will be postponed until the compilation of textbooks for public schools is completed, and then will continue. It is also heard that regarding the compilation of textbooks for public schools, the Ministry plans to review and criticize in detail the textbooks for public schools that have been collected from various provinces and cities, extract the good parts, and organize and supplement them, and the Ministry will compile a kind of textbooks for public schools in order to be universally applicable in various provinces and cities. It is planned to be completed within the year. This organization and compilation work has been designated to be carried out by Zhang Jiong, Director of the Social Education Department, Section Chiefs Ling Xiu and Xu Yiqiao, Commissioner Li Jiaxiang, and Supervisors Tang Xifen and Zhou Bangdao.

Yang Jie Lectures on the Principles of National Establishment of European Powers at Jinling University 200

Jinling University in the capital invited Yang Jie, the current president of the Army University, to give a one-hour lecture on "The Principles of National Establishment of European Powers" at the General Manager's Memorial Week on the 15th. Yang Jie had just returned from a tour of Europe and must have gained a lot of knowledge about the current situation and all the facilities of European countries. First, he made a clear and different comparison of the moral concepts of the East and the West. He said that the national concept of the Atlantic Ocean is "helping the strong and destroying the weak," which is based on a principle of "survival of the fittest." Whoever has cannons, airplanes, and tanks is the most respected. However, the East, such as China, has always advocated "supporting the weak and suppressing the strong." He used the rise of the powers and the current international situation to prove the advantages and disadvantages of these two concepts. Finally, he said that if our country wants to become strong, it must change its political concepts and political methods and catch up with the principles of national establishment of European powers, which can achieve rapid results.

Jiangxi Province's First Women's Games Open Qian Hangsu Performs 50 Meters in 6.8 Seconds and Hurdles in 14.6 Seconds 214

(Nanchang Correspondent) Chairman Chiang takes strengthening the national physique as the center of national rejuvenation, so under Jiang's earnest instructions, the sports atmosphere in Jiangxi is extremely strong. Mr. Village Chief (28) 217

— Wang Renshu

"A'Zhao was beaten to death by you! A'Zhao was beaten to death by you! I don't want dead bones, I want a living A'Zhao! A'Zhao went out alive, how could you replace him with dead bones!"

The woman cried and cried, then suddenly rolled onto the ground again.

A'Zhao's younger brother, A'Ji, looking like a ghost, followed his sister-in-law in. He said, panting:

"My brother was killed by bandits, and now the reserve team has carried his corpse to the entrance of the village. Because they couldn't find the village police, they came to my house."

"Bandits?" Everyone exclaimed in surprise. "What's going on?"

"Yes, bandits." A'Ji yawned, as if he hadn't had enough opium, and said, "This morning, the Black Early team told more than a dozen of them to go to the city to buy vegetables. Each person carried a bamboo pole on their back, like a gun barrel. Things happened to coincide. But then again, there have never been no bandits in the countryside. Now it's getting worse and worse. They walked to Xia Du Village, which is only ten miles away from Lion's Roar Rock. The bandits knew that there were reserve soldiers or something there. When they saw these dozen or so guys carrying bamboo poles on their backs, they thought the reserve soldiers were coming to suppress their bandits. They took these dozen people by surprise and fired a volley of guns, killing four or five people! My brother was shot in the chest and killed!..."

A'Ji spoke and spoke! Finally, his legs seemed unable to support him, and he squatted down on a stone in front of the threshold.

"I want a living person! I want a living person!" A'Zhao's wife was still rolling on the ground.

"This is fate! This is destiny!" Mr. Dasheng shook his head. "I think, I think, the district will always have some compensation!"

"I don't want any compensation! I don't want it! I want a living person! I want a living person! A living, living person!" A'Zhao's wife dragged on the feet of Village Chief Feng Wen.

New York Stock Traders Adopt a Wait-and-See Attitude 231

A report from the Xinfeng Foreign Firm states that yesterday (the 15th), the New York stock market saw sluggish trading and slightly mixed prices. This was due to mixed commercial news, with traders awaiting clarification on monetary conditions and silver prices, adopting a wait-and-see approach. This was caused by China's imposition of an export tax on silver. However, silver stocks rose due to the soaring silver prices. The rise in silver prices was attributed to the belief that the tax would create a shortage of silver in the global market, leading to significant short covering. The bond market was mixed, with strong demand for U.S. government bonds. Stocks on smaller exchanges trended lower. Chicago wheat fell due to weakness in Canadian wheat, which in turn weakened due to large sales from rural areas. The total trading volume was 510,000 shares. Grains: Impact of Soaring Gold Prices: Flour and Wheat Surge in the Afternoon 232

▲ Slight Declines Seen in the Morning

Flour: Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, foreign wheat prices were quoted lower, and various mills rushed to sell, causing the market to decline suddenly. The mills showed a strong intention to sell, totaling no less than 500,000 bags. As a result, market sentiment weakened, and morning closing prices saw a slight drop of two to three cents. However, the imposition of a silver tax led to a reduction in the fineness of foreign gold dollars, causing gold prices to rise. This made foreign wheat less cost-effective. Outside speculators were the first to become bullish, and those covering short positions followed suit with purchases, causing the market to rebound sharply. Major buyers from the Beiyang group and individual investors also made purchases, causing prices for all months to jump by six or seven cents. Compared to the previous day's closing prices, October rose by 2.75 cents, November by 4.5 cents, December by 4.75 cents, January by 3.75 cents, and February by 4 cents.

Wheat: Yesterday, at the opening of the wheat market in the morning, major players closed out long positions. With weak demand from current wheat mills, brokers continued to sell on the exchange, causing prices for all months to fall by four or five cents. In the afternoon, the flour market rose, and the reduction in fineness of U.S. gold dollars caused gold prices to rise, making foreign wheat more expensive. As a result, short sellers stopped selling, and long players stopped closing positions, leading to absorption by new buyers both inside and outside the industry. The market then changed suddenly, with prices soaring beyond expectations. Only near-term months were affected by wheat inventories, lacking the sharpness of far-month gains. However, the final closing price for October was still up by two cents, November by one cent, and December and February by four cents each, while January was up by five cents. Current wheat mills held firm, and only three cars of Shandong wheat were offered on the market at a price of 3.45 yuan, which was purchased by Fuxin.

The Chicago wheat market was initially firm but then faced heavy selling pressure. Additionally, Winnipeg was weak, causing prices to fall. However, conditions in the southwestern producing areas remained dry. Considering the current situation, prices are expected to rise.

Sugar Market: Raw and White Sugar Soar by Two Jiao 234

Yesterday, the sugar market was driven by a sudden increase of over 40 yuan in the gold standard and a rise of one jiao in customs duties, reaching 1.935. This led to a sudden tightening of the trend. The association quoted 18.2 yuan for ordinary spot raw and white sugar, up two jiao from the previous day (14th). Goods in the warehouse and for delivery at the docks were both priced at 18.3 yuan. Re-export goods were priced at 5.3 yuan, up one jiao. High-quality Dutch red sugar was priced at 13.8 yuan, and ordinary at 13.6 yuan. Re-export goods were quoted at 4.8 yuan, a slight increase of one jiao. Locally produced refined white sugar, which had been declining for a long time, also rose by half a jiao on the opportunity of the rebound in raw and white sugar prices, with Zhenyu No. 1 at 16.8 yuan and Zhenji No. 1 quoted at 17 yuan. Domestic green and red sugar prices remained steady, observing the situation as foreign goods rose. If foreign sugar rises further, there is a possibility of following suit.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Speculations and Predictions Regarding "World War" 235

— Jia Wei

Humans living in this era, in this world, are just like sailing boats trying to cross a sea with a rising storm. These sailing boats, of different sizes and ages, are divided into upper and lower classes that are "incompatible like ice and charcoal." Inevitably, internal contradictions arise from their respective interests. What they are crossing is the sea of "history," stirred up by the raging winds of "global economic panic" and the violent waves of "World War II"... Look! What is conspicuously displayed here is a picture and microcosm of this "time" and "space"!

Just like the great human massacre that began in 1914 and lasted for several years, it can give us humans a great lesson. However, less than twenty years after it subsided, all kinds of contradictions and crises are lurking again. Therefore, although the predictions and speculations of general "prophets" and "astrologers" about the timing and location of the "crisis" outbreak are sometimes simply based on no facts, they do indeed indicate the turbulent restlessness of this era and world. Take the so-called "1936 crisis"! More than a year ago, countries were already shouting it to the skies, and people were panicking. Even just the Japanese imperialists, who lit the fuse of the Far East powder keg, have published more than a dozen books on the "1936" problem, as far as I personally have seen. Moreover, Japanese imperialists are using "radio stations" every day to broadcast this "1936" impending disaster to stir up the "patriotic thoughts" of the general lower classes, preparing them to become "human bullets" for the motherland in the future. But looking back at our country, from January to July of this year, the total value of wireless machine imports was more than 1.4 million gold yuan. However, every day they are sending you soul-stirring songs like "Taohuajiang is a Beauty's Nest...", "Sweet Dreams...", "I Don't Want Your Gold, I Only Want Your Heart...", and "×× Opening...", "This Company's New Arrival ×× Goods..." This is enough to show the "national sentiment" of the leisure class.

However, the "1936" crisis is not accidental or without cause. The "global economic panic" after 1928, the "1918" incident, Japan's withdrawal from the "League of Nations," the fruitless "Disarmament Conference," the expiration of the "Naval Treaty" in 1935, etc., are all direct causes and starting points of this "crisis"! Although, the timing will not be so rigid!

Reading yesterday's newspaper, a telegram from New York, someone is predicting a "world war" again. It is said that this is a "person known for his familiarity with the German situation," "and Mr. Steele, who was able to predict Hitler's cleansing movement two weeks in advance." Today, he predicted again that "World War II" will occur next year, and said that the outbreak of war cannot be delayed beyond the summer of 1935, because Germany will no longer be able to pay France under the Treaty of Versailles. Therefore, it is necessary to occupy the Saar to reclaim the region's rich coal and iron mines. At that time, Japanese imperialism will take advantage of the chaos in Europe to attack the Soviet Union to maintain its economic hegemony in the Far East.

Originally, today, we all must know: when the "global economic panic" and "international political crisis" have reached their peak, the second great human massacre is bound to descend upon the world! The important thing is: how will we humans, each riding in a crisis-ridden sailing boat, annihilate the "internal contradictions" and follow this historical route to weather the shocking and turbulent storms?

Page 18

Autumn Harvest 236

— Chao Ren

A Yuan, why is your rent rice always delayed? Last year was a famine year, and I let you delay it until the end of the year. This year's autumn harvest is not bad. None of the tenant farmers go to the warehouse to pay clearly. Are you planning to delay even longer? Be sensible, and settle it quickly to save us from making extra trips.

Uncle, I'm really sorry for making you come all this way. I'll pour you some tea to moisten your mouth. Please sit down and rest for a while.

Of course I'll sit down. I came all the way for you. Don't be long-winded. Just take the money out. That's taking care of people.

A Yuan poured a cup of steaming strong tea from the teapot, but he was planning in his heart how to deal with the current predicament. Hearing the increasingly urgent urging, his heart also became increasingly panicked. But, looking at his child's yellow face and the empty rice bucket, he still mustered up hope to plead.

I should have come to pay the rent earlier, but this year's harvest was not good either. There was a drought for more than twenty days. You uncle knows that. Although there was some rain afterwards, most of the seedlings had already withered. Fortunately, I still planted in the low-lying fields.

Stop it. There's no need to say more. Anyway, it can't be considered a famine year. If I let you off just by saying a few empty words, then in the future, tenants wouldn't need to prepare silver dollars. They would just need a mouth that can talk.

What you say is true, and sooner or later I have to pay it off, but I really can't scrape it together now. I hope you uncle can help me out by giving me a few more days.

Humph! What kind of times are these? All the deadlines have passed. You simply want to eat rent rice. To put it bluntly, eating rent rice is against the law. There's nothing else to say. Hurry up and take the money out, or else I won't have anything to tell Li Zhonglao when I go back, and I won't be able to be lenient. Zhonglao's business card is already here. I'll take you to the Public Security Bureau.

A Yuan was extremely panicked at this time. He knew Li's landlord's power. Many tenants had been sent to the Public Security Bureau for owing rent, but he didn't have a single penny. What could he do? Worrying wouldn't help. His heart suddenly relaxed. Anyway, he couldn't escape his fate. He would stand up and go with the rent collector.

Okay, so be it if I get sued. I really can't squeeze out any money. It's fine if you uncle takes me to the city.

The cunning rent collector didn't expect him to finally become tough. It was a pity that all his threats were in vain. Although sending a tenant who owes rent to the authorities was very reasonable, he also understood A Yuan's predicament. Empty threats couldn't squeeze out any money. It was better to give him a few more days to raise the money. Just for the sake of dignity, he couldn't directly soften his tone.

You make it sound easy. Lawsuits aren't easy to handle. Who will take care of your family if you go to jail? I think you should think of another way.

Who wants to go to jail? Alas, since you uncle is looking after me, I wonder if you can give me a few more days.

You have to understand that we also used other people's money and can't help but do this. We don't like to make enemies with people. Since that's the case, forcing you won't get me any money. Now I'm specially giving you three more days. If I don't get an explanation after three days, then I'll have to be impolite.

Thank you very much. I will definitely try my best to find a way in three days.

Remember, if you don't pay the money after three days, I'll really have to deal with you.

These were the words the rent collector said as he left, as if to show the seriousness of his business. A Yuan was worried in his heart: what explanation would he have if he didn't have any money after three days? He looked at the rice bucket and could only sigh.

Three days will pass very quickly, he looked at his son's yellow face.

A Late Autumn Night's Note 237

— Jing Yun

The night has deepened, and the alley is as silent as stagnant water. There are no sounds of vendors selling snacks, and the children living together are all quietly lying in bed, enjoying their sweet dreams. At this moment, I am sitting facing the yellow light, propping up my thin chin, thinking about the topic of the article.

Calligraphy by Mr. Xu Cihua 238

Village Studio Falls Into Talking Knot Table Bamboo For

Divine Clarity and Harmony Write Fragrance With the Moon

Trap Smoke Also Some Trees Saint Remnant Charm For Flowers Without Such Posture Poet's Demeanor Like Dreams Also Courtyard Thoughts

Autumn Day of Jiaxu [Year]

Xu Cihua

Suddenly, a sharp gust of cold wind whistled in through the window, icy cold. Through the extremely thin pajamas, it made me shiver a few times. Thus, I deeply felt that autumn had deepened.

Autumn may be considered by people to be an extremely beautiful and poetic season! Fat crabs, slender chrysanthemums, half a catty of yellow wine, drinking alone in front of the moon. When I am tipsy, I stand up and sing at the top of my lungs, forgetting heaven and earth and forgetting myself, living a semi-hermitic life. If, in the quiet of the night, I wake up from a new dream and listen to the sparse rain tapping on the remaining lotus leaves, the so-called "keeping the remaining lotus to listen to the sound of rain," how much does this scene and feeling suit the tastes of poets? Then, it is not impossible to temporarily be a poet.

Autumn is truly a beautiful and extremely poetic season!

Every morning, I sit up from bed and flip through the newly delivered newspapers. The most eye-catching things are the autumn sales advertisements of major companies and the forest of tempting, excellent films in the movie theaters. Indeed, this autumn season is much better than the scorching summer. It is so comfortable to sit on a soft cotton sofa! At the same time, I no longer smell that kind of nauseating, salty and sour sweaty smell. Especially those coquettish and graceful women seem even more graceful and lovely in this clear and refreshing autumn.

However, these are the comforts and joys that only a very small number of people can get from autumn. Under the double pressure of natural and man-made disasters, the autumn harvest that farmers have been looking forward to has been abandoned. Watching their old home丨the countryside丨go bankrupt faster and faster day by day, even the problem of eating has caused panic, what leisure do they have to appreciate this beautiful and poetic autumn like those poets who have nothing to do after eating their fill! Moreover, the weather is getting colder day by day. Aren't all their winter clothes for keeping out the cold sent to the pawnshop? But, the autumn harvest is already hopeless. What ability do they have to get those winter clothes for keeping out the cold from the pawnshop? Thinking of the harsh winter, these poor people began to worry about the cool autumn that was quietly descending on the world.

Terrifying autumn! Perhaps you are the executioner who controls the fate of the poor.

Vaguely, I seem to hear those homeless poor people, on the streets in the middle of the night, soaking in the rustling autumn wind, constantly shivering, and sighing quietly...

"These are all unfortunate people adrift in the world! After a deep breath, a sigh of sympathy.

Amateur Mailbox

Mortgage Collateral Expires and Loses Value 239

To the Editor:

I am a resident of Wuyuan County in Anhui Province. I have a difficult matter that I have been contemplating for months without a resolution. Therefore, I am compelled to seek your assistance in finding a solution.

Three years ago, when a younger relative of mine was getting married, I was asked to borrow several hundred yuan from various sources on his behalf. The loan agreement stipulated that the principal and interest would be repaid when the fir trees in the countryside were sold. According to the calculations at that time, the timber price would have been more than sufficient to cover the debt. However, due to the recent rural economic downturn and financial ruin, timber merchants who transport wood to Zhejiang and Hangzhou have reduced the timber prices due to a lack of sales channels. Recently, there has been almost no demand. As a result, the agreement to settle the debt with timber prices cannot be fulfilled, and the interest is increasing daily. If I declare bankruptcy, there are no lawyers in the countryside to handle the liquidation, and self-assessment and distribution are not permitted by the creditors. This situation is quite perplexing. I earnestly request your assistance in finding a solution. With respectful greetings.

Sincerely, Xin Jiu

Editor's Note: According to the letter, Mr. Xin Jiu does not seem to be the guarantor, and therefore has no legal responsibility. However, since the matter was handled previously, it is morally appropriate to help resolve it.

The first step is to investigate whether there is any possibility of the mortgaged property increasing in value. At the same time, convene all creditors for sincere consultation. If there is no chance of the mortgaged property increasing in value and the loan is due, the mortgaged property must first be sold. The amount not covered should then be negotiated for a repayment schedule, and the debtor should find a way to raise the funds.

My Job Seeking Advertisement

Ms. Wan, from Jiangsu, a graduate of a normal school, has worked as a school teacher, tutor, and scribe for many years. She is now seeking the above or other positions. Correspondence address: c/o Ms. Yang, No. 11, Lane 185, Rue G. Kahn, French Concession.

News 243

The China Harmonica Music Score Publishing House, located at 110 Renji Road in this city, in order to arouse the interest of harmonica music lovers nationwide, will hold a song guessing competition starting from the 16th of this month. The method of guessing involves the selection of ten famous harmonica songs by the publishing house, pre-arranging their order, and sealing them for display in the windows of the Kaiming Bookstore Author's Society on Fuzhou Road and the Gangyue Huamei Electrical Appliance Store on Nanjing Road, to ensure fairness. It is reported that the announcement date has been set for 11:00 AM on November 11th, when the top ten songs will be unsealed in public at each display location. At the same time, the top ten songs will be announced to the nation via the Huamei Radio Station, and the Public Harmonica Research Association will be invited to broadcast these famous songs to enhance the event. Those who wish to participate in the competition can fill in the arranged order of the top ten songs on the guessing competition ticket provided by the publishing house and mail it to the publishing house, sealed, before 12:00 PM on November 10th. Those whose guesses match the announced order will receive valuable prizes from the publishing house, and those who do not guess correctly will also receive a song score. Detailed guessing instructions are posted at each display location, along with the titles of the top ten songs:

General Boulanger March, Orpheus in the Underworld, La Paloma, The Happy Blacksmith, Moonlight Fantasia, Aida, Fate, Carmen, Spring Slumber Song, The Merry Widow.
