Shen Bao Local Supplement Car Weekly

New Trends in 1935 Model Cars 244

— Zhen Min

The 1934 model cars, at first glance, seem perfect in terms of structure, appearance, and performance. However, after careful study by engineers from various countries, many shortcomings were discovered, such as the lack of a standard format for vehicles and the outdated ventilation in the cabins. Everything awaited improvement by engineers. Now, the newly born 1935 model cars have advantages that exceed our expectations, far surpassing the old 1934 models. The first reason why the 1935 model cars have achieved such success and are considered ideal vehicles is, of course, due to the reduction of automobile taxes by the governments of various countries (England, America, France) (a 20% reduction). This light tax change is enough to increase the purchasing power of small horsepower car owners. For example, those who originally bought 14 horsepower cars can now buy 18 or 20 horsepower cars. This change in horsepower directly provides car factories with more advanced designs and manufacturing, allowing engineers to conduct deeper research and produce excellent car engines. This is undoubtedly true.

The price increase is directly proportional to the cost of raw materials. In recent years, the prices of various raw materials have been rising sharply, so the price of the 1935 model cars will be at least a little more expensive than the old cars. This is also unavoidable.

In the 1934 model cars, we can see various different and strange-looking cars, such as rocket-shaped and olive-shaped cars. However, this phenomenon will absolutely not be found in the 1935 model cars, because engineers agree that these strange-shaped vehicles are an expression of car factories showing off to their peers. As a result, the construction of the engine and body is often perfunctory, failing to achieve excellent results. Therefore, the 1935 model cars belong to the condition of "standardization." Factories are striving for the precision and solidity of the body construction, abandoning external competition.

Independent spring suspension was slightly adopted in the 1934 model cars, but there was no standard, and no complete testing was conducted. The results were naturally inferior. The 1935 model cars are different. Even small springs have undergone static and dynamic testing. The vibration amplitude after the engine starts is reduced to a minimum. The front and rear axle supports are equipped with vibration-absorbing interlayer rubber springs. Even when driving on rough roads, the cabin does not experience severe jolting.

The connection of the car cabin has been studied by many engineers in recent years, and satisfactory results have finally been achieved. The 1935 model cars have all adopted it. The car windows are made of two layers of glass. The inner layer can be raised and lowered freely, and the outer layer is equipped with a pivot, which can be pushed outwards to any angle. In this way, air circulation is completely around the car cabin, greatly reducing resistance and air pressure.

The length of the new cars is about 20% greater than the old cars, and the width is about 10% greater. The degree of streamlining is roughly similar to the old cars, but it is more even.

Although the increase in tire cross-section was blindly opposed by many engineers in the past, it has now been a great success. The total tire air volume of the 1935 model cars is 5-7% higher than the old cars, thus increasing the load by 23-30%. These results are quite astonishing.

The connection of the rotating parts of this car all use the latest roller system. The frictional force of the metal area is naturally reduced. Each shaft part has an automatic lubricator to inject lubricating oil. When there is excess lubricating oil, it can flow back to the central lubrication system at an extremely fast rate, with absolutely no leakage or other losses. The braking of the engine utilizes the latest electromagnetic coil induction. Any external temperature has no effect. The control of voltage and the distribution of electricity are managed by precision machinery. Therefore, the ability and efficiency of the electric motor are exceptionally high. This is also a feature of the 1935 model cars.

In short, although the price of the new cars is slightly higher, the reduction in car tax excites the car factories to manufacture, so there are such achievements. These "standardized" new cars will soon be sold in the car market and warmly welcomed by the general public. This is undoubtedly true.

Road Safety Issues 245

— Fu

Advice from Experts

Mr. Jings, a famous skilled car driver, holds the American Automobile Association records for various competitions regarding distance, speed, and endurance. The number of records he has created is so large that other drivers can only look on in amazement, with no one able to match him. What is even more commendable is that, although he has repeatedly set the highest records, he has never caused an accident. Recently, he provided six points of advice regarding road safety issues, which were published in the newly published Rotary magazine. I have translated them below for the reference of those who are concerned about car driving safety.

(1) Always Manage the Steering Wheel with Both Hands: As far as I know, there are skilled drivers who use one hand, but it is better to manage the steering wheel with both hands.

(2) Fit the Best Tires on the Front Wheels: Front tire blowouts are more dangerous. If a blowout unfortunately occurs, only by firmly gripping the steering wheel can danger be avoided.

(3) Always Check the Brakes: After I start driving, I always step on the foot pedal within the first 100 yards to check the brakes, because the brakes may be frozen, sticky, or in need of adjustment.

(4) Drive Even More Carefully When the Sky is Dim: When driving fast at dawn or dusk, the possibility of causing an accident will be many times greater than in the morning or daytime. The reason for this is, of course, due to unclear visibility. We must also remember that fatal car crash cases increase by 42% at night compared to daytime.

(5) It is not necessary to use the brakes when coasting.

(6) Always Pay Attention to Road Conditions.

The Progress of Dodge Cars in the Last Twenty Years 246

— Ying Dai

The Dodge factory, as we all know, has a very long history in the automotive industry. 1934 marks the 20th anniversary of the Dodge factory. In the past twenty years, the Dodge factory has made significant progress. And now, Dodge's products are renowned in the automotive industry. The position it occupies in the automotive industry is getting higher and higher day by day. Today, it is qualified to be a leader. The only reason why Dodge has such a position today is the stability of the factory's business policies and the excellence of its products. Therefore, the history of the Dodge factory for twenty years is the entire history of the development of Dodge cars.

The superiority of the Dodge six-cylinder car is the result of efforts to improve it over the past twenty years. And "buoyancy" is a special achievement among various inventions and improvements. The Dodge car body is made entirely of single-piece pure steel. Therefore, the general public has recognized the Dodge car body as one of the safest car bodies. Safety glass provides drivers and passengers with great safety. And in this year's new cars, the most significant reform is the independent suspension of the front wheels. With the device of independent suspension, the vehicle can avoid all tilting and backward shaking force when driving on the road. As a result, it can give any car owner unexpected safety and speed.

In terms of ventilation, the invention and adoption of a new type of windless ventilation system is more advanced than any ventilation system ever used on Dodge cars. With this new device, the windows can be completely lowered, including the ventilation part and independent ventilation. The engine on the six-cylinder Dodge car, operated by a crank on the dashboard, is huge and powerful, and very glossy. Now, a seven-point weighted crank rod is used. Just these points can make us feel that Dodge's new cars have made significant progress in form and mechanism.

The streamline of the 1934 Dodge six-cylinder car is not only long and low, but also very balanced. The padding and decoration, everything, is beautiful and modern. The style is very good, whether inside or outside the car. In terms of structure, the car body is made of single-piece pure steel, so it is like a steel boat hull, using the welding method, so there are no cracks at the seams, so it is safe and strong. It is unmatched by the car bodies of any new cars. Steel inside and steel outside is the most solid kind of vehicle in the 1934 new cars.

In addition to passenger cars, the Dodge factory is also famous for manufacturing trucks. This is also well known. The Dodge factory has also been manufacturing trucks for eighteen years. In the process of manufacturing trucks, the Dodge factory has always considered the industrial sector, so that they can save money by purchasing Dodge trucks. With rich experience, until now, everyone has recognized that the products can indeed surpass their material excellence and engineering convenience. The manufacturing technology is very skillful and exquisite. All equipment is also readily available. Therefore, after the industrial sector adopts Dodge freight trucks, we can guarantee that their expenses will definitely be reduced a lot, because the transportation is fast and easy. Whether in terms of fuel, maintenance costs, or the original investment, it will feel very economical.

Public Concession Autumn Automobile Registration Statistics 248

— Pei

From July 1st to September 30th. The statistics for the third quarter of this year for automobile registrations in the Public Concession have been published. The number of various automobiles registered is greater than in the summer of this year. The totals are: (1) Automobile license plates: 155 types, 6,794 private automobiles, 510 public automobiles, totaling 7,304. (2) Goods vehicle license plates: 143 types, 1,180 private goods vehicles, 864 public goods vehicles, 164 public passenger buses, totaling 2,208. (3) Motorcycle license plates: 57 types, 691 motorcycles.

The number of automobile registrations in the Public Concession in the autumn of 1934 increased compared to the summer of this year. A comparison of the summer and autumn seasons is as follows: (1) Number of automobiles: 7,304 in autumn, 7,136 in summer. (2) Goods vehicles slightly decreased in autumn compared to summer. The number of registrations from April to June was 2,222, and from July to September it was 2,208. (3) Motorcycle statistics for autumn were also inferior to summer. There were 768 in summer and 691 in autumn. All of the above statistics do not include military vehicles.

French Highway Construction 250

— Shelley

Building Five New Automobile Roads

Recently, the French government prepared to take 10,000,000,000 francs for road improvement expenses. The method of allocating all of this huge expense has also been decided. Half of this funding is used to build new road networks that connect to the outside of Paris and for road construction in the Paris area. The other half is used to improve highways throughout France, and the most important thing is to eliminate level crossings everywhere.

It seems like a large expense to use half of the total funding for the construction and improvement of roads in Paris. However, we must know that in France, the important highways, needless to say, are in very good condition on most of the secondary roads. Therefore, apart from the special goals mentioned, there is actually no need for huge expenditures to repair and improve the roads. Because the situation in Paris is completely the opposite of what has been mentioned earlier, urgent repairs and improvements are very important. The traffic congestion on the main roads leading to the capital of Paris has reached its peak in recent years. This summer, if it is a Saturday or Sunday, the congestion on the roads often extends for many miles. The traffic obstruction can be imagined. The plan to improve roads in Paris includes the construction of five major automobile roads spreading out from the city center and connecting with the ring roads in the suburbs. It is reported that the construction of three of the five highways will start soon.

The three major roads mentioned above are the Great Western Road, the Great Southern Road, and the Northern Road. Because Paris is geographically the intersection of continental air routes, the Northern Road leads directly to the Bourget Airport. The starting point of the Southern Road will be between the existing roads to Arpajon and Fontainebleau. Vehicle traffic is currently very congested on these two roads. The Arpajon Road mentioned above leads directly to Orléans and Bordeaux. The Fontainebleau line goes directly to Lyon and southern France.

Whether it is day or night, vehicle traffic is very congested on the roads mentioned above. However, the situation is even more complicated near Paris, because most of the suburban vehicle traffic consists of cargo vehicles. Doesn't this make vehicle traffic even more troublesome? If the newly opened roads are completed, then the aforementioned traffic congestion difficulties will not be difficult to resolve, because the plan is to extend the new roads 20 miles outside of Paris and then connect them with the existing roads.

The new Western Road will start in Husine. You can reach the bridge from Bronchi and connect with the Le Portes Cardi road, extending directly to western France. It also connects with the Pondorsdiperes Road. In addition to the two roads above, the third major road is shorter but very important. This road will extend from Bobigny to connect Paris with the Northern (Chantilly) Road. In this way, we will have the fastest ground transportation between Paris and the various important airports.

In addition to the new spider web network, there are many road construction projects related to Paris itself and its suburbs that are also being planned. There are still many level crossings in the suburbs, which will soon be eliminated. The Seine Bridge will be widened. The traffic congestion caused by the fall of the old fortress line will be resolved.

Because the fall of the Port of Delphi has been significantly successful, the municipal authorities have now begun to add other tunnels, such as the tunnels of Meroude and Jinbailai, which are already known. The completion of these is not far away. It is expected that one or two of the tunnels will be fully completed next year. At the same time, the problem of traffic congestion will be solved along with it. Vehicle traffic from Meroude in and out of Paris has always been very complex, especially on weekends, which is even more difficult to solve.

A new tunnel at Fanlitot Port has been under construction for a long time and will definitely be

Page 23

completed and opened this year. In this way, ground traffic to Bobigny Airport can be diverted. There are also two tunnels of the same nature under construction, one in Italy and one in Crete. These two places have always been concentrated points of traffic congestion. However, there is still a tunnel being planned, which will be built under the Seine beach at Carrousel Port.

Efforts are being made to use tunnels to solve the difficulty of complex traffic, not only in the city but also in the suburbs. The idea is to use tunnels to eliminate level crossings in the suburbs, and the traffic underneath is railway traffic rather than road traffic. The intersections of Bushkolombers and Akishi are two good examples. There used to be three level crossings in that area within 100 yards. After passing through one gate, car drivers would continuously face the second gate in the short lane. The first gate had closed behind the car, as if it were a cow or a sheep, closed in a fence. It would take at least twenty-five minutes, or even longer, to pass through.

The municipal engineering of France is very developed. Therefore, the improvements to the difficulties and complexities mentioned above can be effectively demonstrated.

Talking About Changes in Automobile Styles 251

— Zhongqin

Automobiles have recently been regarded not only as a means of transportation, but also as a beautiful and magnificent object. Because automobiles are regarded as a beautiful and magnificent object, general automobile dealers are doing their best to improve the beauty of the appearance, and the beauty of the appearance is the issue of automobile style. This is probably one of the most important things about automobiles today. If a car buyer notices the style of the car first when buying a car,

If he is an automobile manufacturing expert, in his words, he can often hear things like the 1930 style, the 1933 style, or the 1934 style. It can be seen that style is the most important condition for automobiles today. Automobile styles change every year, with new developments every day and month. Therefore, general automobile manufacturers are doing their best to seek improvements. This improvement has caused a trend of change in automobile styles, gradually changing from one style to another.

If we are talking about large cars, then there are styles of large cars. Because the world today is a world of economic panic, all trends are heading towards the economic side. Therefore, automobiles have to tend towards economy. For example, Austin automobiles, originally famous for small cars, are carrying out their reform policy during this period, making small cars active on the market. Star cars also launched fresh small cars at the same time. Ford cars also have new styles of small cars appearing on the market. Other Niu, Hillman, Nash and other cars also have the latest styles of small cars. It can be seen that this is a general trend. All automobile manufacturing industries are affected by this trend during this period.

However, in terms of the general changes in automobile styles, that applies to both large and small cars. Ten years ago, the style of automobiles was to advocate high car bodies and shorter lengths. At that time, all automobiles were very expensive. Because the car body was high, the chassis below was also raised accordingly. The corners of the car body were angular, because at that time, the idea was to make the square corner beautiful, so all the roof corners were square. Such a car was very fashionable at that time. Of course, this same car cannot be found in any automobile factory now, and if there is such a vehicle on the market, it must be considered very ugly. However, ten years ago, this style was considered the most beautiful among automobiles. A few can still be found, like old Lincoln cars and Packard cars, which are still very solid, but the car body style is very old. It is still visible on the market. Although the style is very ugly, the value of this car is very expensive.
